
1a1(rgyud 'grel): gnod sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi sbyor ka chen po'i cho ga sta stabs kyi sbyor ka ste sum cu bzhi pa'o//
1b1(rgyud 'grel): rgya gar skad du/ mahA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni ma hA ga na bid+hi/ bod skad du/ gnod
1b2(rgyud 'grel): sbyin gyi sde dpon chen po lag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sbyor ka chen po'i cho ga /bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gos sngon
1b3(rgyud 'grel): po can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dus gsum bder gshegs thams cad kyis/ /rig sngags gsang sngags bdag po ru/ /
1b4(rgyud 'grel): dbang bskur 'byung po tshar gcod pa/ /gsang sngags sdud mdzad khyod phyag 'tshal/ /bcom ldan phyag na rdo rje yi/ /rgyud
2a1(rgyud 'grel): rnams ma lus kun dang ni/ /rnal 'byor pha rgyud ma rgyud kyi/ /rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud dang ni/ /rnal 'byor
2a2(rgyud 'grel): rgyud dang spyod pa'i rgyud/ /rgyud rnams kun dang mi 'gal phyir/ /man ngag cung zad dran pa 'di/ /blo dman bsgrub pa'i don du
2a3(rgyud 'grel): ni/ /rnal 'byor cha rkyen bstan par bya/ /sbyor ba'i rim pa dpag med kyang/ /sgrub pa po yi don slad du/ /dgos pa bsdus
2a4(rgyud 'grel): pa bstan pa 'di/ /sgrub po slob dpon dang bral na/ /sbyor ba 'di rnams bstan par gsungs/ /de la sbyor ba rim bzhin bstan//
2b1(rgyud 'grel): dang po tshogs gnyis rdzogs bya'i phyir/ /bdag nyid skad cig lhar sprul la/ /snying gar zla ba'i maN+Dal bsam/ /hUM gi 'od zer 'phros pa las/
2b2(rgyud 'grel): sgrib pa sbyangs nas phyi nang gsal/ /mdun du zla ba'i gzugs brnyan dang/ /pad+ma'i gzugs brnyan gsum mam gcig /la la gzhal yas
2b3(rgyud 'grel): sprul par 'dod/ /de ru dkyil 'khor bsam pa dang/ /bsod nams don phyir spyan drangs bstim/ /bla ma sbyang sogs byas nas kyang/ /gzhan
2b4(rgyud 'grel): sogs man ngag bzhin du bya/ /phyag 'tshal phyi nang gsang bas mchod/ /mtshams med mi dge sdom nyams nas/ /rtsa ba'i dam tshig nyams
2b5(rgyud 'grel): pa kun/ /sgyu ma'i sems kyis bshags par bya/ /dge ba kun la rjes yi rang/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar bskul/ /mya ngan mi 'da' gsol
3a1(rgyud 'grel): ba 'debs/ /rdo rje can la skyabs su mchi/ /rdo rje can la lus 'bul lo/ /bsod nams ci bsags thams cad kun/ /byang chub
3a2(rgyud 'grel): chen por bsngo bar bya/ /tshad med bzhi yang bsgom par bya/ /de nas phyi nang snod bcud kun/ /stong pa nyid du bsgom par bya/ /de nas nam mkha' i chos 'byung la/ /
3a3(rgyud 'grel): yi ge cho 'phrul 'phros pa las/ /'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor rim bzhin bskyed/ /de yi steng du ri rab bskyed/ /de steng rdo rje rgya gram la/ /'khor lo rtsibs
3a4(rgyud 'grel): bcu 'bar bas mtshan/ /zla ba'i steng du gnod mdzes sprul/ /yi ge hUM gi 'phro 'du las/ /khro bo bcu sprul hUM bzhi yi/ /gsang sngags bzlas nas
3a5(rgyud 'grel): bka' bsgo bya/ /khro bo sprul pas bgegs rnams bkug /yang bsgo sku gsung thugs kyi ni/ /phur bu'i sngags brjod tho bas brdung/ /bsregs nas
3b1(rgyud 'grel): nam mkha' nyid du 'gyur/ /de nas hUM gi 'phro 'du yis/ /rdo rje gur dang ra bar 'gyur/ /yi ge b+h+ruM gyi 'phro 'du las/ /gnod mdzes 'od du zhu nas kyang/ /gzhal yas khang ni mdzes par 'gyur//
3b2(rgyud 'grel): de steng pad+ma 'dab brgyad gdan/ /rang gi sems kyi tshe 'phrul las/ /zla ba'i dkyil 'khor chen po la/ /yi ge A lis mtshan bar bya/ /nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po la/ /yi ge kA lis
3b3(rgyud 'grel): mtshan par bya/ /hUM las rdo rje de nyid mtshan/ /byin brlabs bsdus nas 'od du zhu/ /de las sku ni bskyed par bya/ /pad+ma dbus kyi lte ba la/ /bcom ldan rdo rje gos sngon can/ /shar gyi
3b4(rgyud 'grel): pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/ /khro bo rnam par rgyal ba bskyed/ /lho yi pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/ /bcom ldan mgon po nag po bskyed/ /nub kyi pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/ /lus ngan rgyal po bskyed par bya/ /byang
3b5(rgyud 'grel): gi pad+ma'i 'dab ma la/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil pa bskyed par bya/ /byang shar du ni gnod sbyin bskyed/ /shar lho ru ni ro langs ma/ /lho nub rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/ /nub byang du ni 'jigs byed ma/ /
3b6(rgyud 'grel): mtshams rnams su ni lha mo bzhi/ /'od skyed ma dang yid 'phrog ma/ /kun bzang ma dang glu sgra ma/ /shar gyi sgo ru srog gcod ma/ /lho yi sgo ru dbugs rdub ma/ /nub kyi phyogs su khrag 'thung ma/
4a1(rgyud 'grel): byang gi phyogs su sha za ma/ /de ltar dkyil 'khor bskyed nas kyang/ /yi ge hUM gi 'od zer dang/ /sngags dang phyag rgya'i tshigs bcad sgras/ /rang bzhin dkyil 'khor spyan drangs la/ /mchod bstod
4a2(rgyud 'grel): byas nas dam tshig la/ /byin brlabs bstims te dbang bskur ro/ /de lta'i dkyil 'khor chen po la/ /thun bzhi thun brgyad bar dag tu/ /bsgoms nas brtan par gyur pas na/ /las rnams gzhan nam rdzogs rim
4a3(rgyud 'grel): la/ /gzhug par bya ba kho na yin/ /'khor lo chen po'i sbyor ka ste dang po'o// //bcom ldan rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dkyil 'khor chen po mi nus pas/ /lha rnams so so kun la yang//
4a4(rgyud 'grel): rgyan gcig pa la sbyor ba bstan/ /dang po gtso bo'i sbyor ba ni/ /bdag nyid skad cig lhar sprul la/ /yi ge hUM man ngag sogs/ /rim pa bzhin du shes par bya/ /phyag 'tshal mchod cing bshags pa dang/ /rjes su
4a5(rgyud 'grel): yi rang bskul ba dang/ /gsol ba gdab cing skyabs su gsol/ /lus 'bul dge rtsa bsngo bar bya/ /chad med bzhi bsgom stong nyid bsgom/ /stong pa'i ngang las yi ge hUM/ /de las phyag mtshan rdo rjer gyur/ /de nyid las ni sku bskyed do//
4a6(rgyud 'grel): sku mdog sngon po zhal gcig pa/ /mche ba gtsigs mdzad spyan mig bzlog /phyag g.yas rdo rje bsnams mdzad nas/ /phyag g.yon nam mkha' lding ni bsnams/ /g.yon brkyang g.yas bskum klu la shis/ /g.yas pa rdo rje bsnam mdzad nas/
4b1(rgyud 'grel): g.yon brtse gsum bsnams pa ni/ /gshin rje dag la shis par bstan/ /g.yas pa rdo rje gsor nas ni/ /g.yon pa dril bu bsgrags pa ni/ /gnod sbyin drag la shis par bstan/ /ye shes dkyil 'khor spyan drangs bstim /byin brlabs dbang bskur byas nas kyang/ /thun mtshams
4b2(rgyud 'grel): bzhir ni brtan par bsgom/ /gtso bo'i sbyor ka ste gnyis pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rnam par rgyal ba la phyag 'tshal lo/ /skad cig lhar sbrol thugs ka ru/ /nyi ma'i steng du hUM sogs rdzogs/ /phyag 'tshal mchod cing bshags par bya/ /rjes su yi rang la sogs bya//
4b3(rgyud 'grel): stong pa nyid du bsgoms nas kyang/ /stong pa'i ngang las cho 'phrul du/ /rdo rje pad+ma nyi zla'i steng/ /de steng hUM las rdo rjer gyur/ /rdo rje las ni sku bskyed do/ /khro cha khams gsum rnam rgyal na/ /sku mdog dmar po dbu gsum pa/ /phyag drug dang po rdo rje'o/ /g.yon gyi dang po dgra sta'o/ /bar
4b4(rgyud 'grel): ma gnyis kyis 'ching byed pa/ /gung mo mthe bong ngos btung nas/ /gzhan rnams yongs su brkyang ba yin/ /de nyid snying khar bzung nas ni/ /de 'og g.yas pas zhags pa bsnams/ /g.yon pa ral gri bsnams pa'o/ /ye shes spyan drangs bstims nas kyang/ /byin
4b5(rgyud 'grel): brlabs dbang bskur byas nas ni/ /thun mtshams bzhi ru brtan par bsgom/ /snying kha'i man ngag gsal nas kyang/ /lce ni rdo rjer byin gyis brlabs/ /bzlas brjod 'phros 'dus bsnyen pa bya/ /dus grangs mchan ma thems pa dang/ /bsgrub pa gang 'dod brtsam par bya'o//
4b6(rgyud 'grel): rnam par rgyal ba'i sbyor ka gsum pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das dpal mgon po nag po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /skad cig lha ru sprul nas kyang/ /hUM gi man ngag rdzogs pa yis/ /phyag 'tshal mchod pa la sogs bya/ /stong pa nyid kyi dang nyid las/ /rin chen gdan sogs rdzogs
4b7(rgyud 'grel): byas la/ /yi ge hUM las be tson gyur/ /de nyid las ni sku rdzogs gyur/ /dpal ldan mgon po nag po ni/ /sku mdog nag po dung sprin 'dra/ /zhal gcig pa la phyag gnyis pa/ /g.yas pa tsan dan bde? chen bsnams/ /g.yon pa zhags pa bsnams pa'o/ /zhabs ni brkyan
5a1(rgyud 'grel): bskum tshul du bzhugs/ /ye shes mgon po spyan drangs bstims/ /byin brlabs dbang bskur la sogs bya/ /de ltar bstan nas bzlas brjod bya/ /mgon po mdun du spyan drangs nas/ /bzlas brjod la sogs rdzogs byas la/ /de nas sgrub pa brtsam par bya//
5a2(rgyud 'grel): mgon po las kyi sbyor ka ste bzhi pa'o// //lus ngan gsung mchog sprul la phyag 'tshal lo/ /skad cig lhar sprul hUM gis ni/ /spyan drangs la sogs rdzogs byas la/ /phyag 'tshal mchod pa la sogs bya/ /stong pa'i ngang las pad sogs gang na/ /yi ge hUM las mchod
5a3(rgyud 'grel): rten gyur/ /de nyid las ni sku bskyed do/ /lus ngan sku mdog ljang gu'o/ /zhal gcig phyag g.yas mchod rten bsnams/ /g.yon pa ne'u le bsnams pa'o/ /ye shes spyan drangs bstims nas ni/ /byin gyis brlabs cing dbang bskur ro/ /bzlas brjod bsnyen pa rdzogs nas ni//
5a4(rgyud 'grel): de nas sgrub pa brtsam par bya'o/ /lus ngan po'i sbyor ka ste lnga pa'o// //khro chen bdud rtsi 'khyil la phyag 'tshal lo/ /skad cig lhar sprul hUM gis ni/ /sbyor ba la sogs rdzogs par bya/ /de nas phyag 'tshal mchod sogs bya/ /stong ba'i ngang las rdo rje'i gdan/ /de
5a5(rgyud 'grel): steng hUM las rdo rje'o/ /de nyid las ni sku rdzogs 'gyur/ /khro chen bdud rtsi 'khyil pa sku sngon po/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis brang du bsnol/ zhabs gnyis brkyang bskum tshul du bzhugs/ /ye shes dkyil 'khor spyan drangs bstim/ /byin gyis brlab cing dbang
5a6(rgyud 'grel): bskur ro/ /bsnyen pa la sogs rdzogs nas ni/ /de nas bsgrub pa brtsam par bya'o/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sbyor ka ste drug pa'o// //mkha' 'gro ma rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gnod sbyin mkha' 'gro la sogs kyang/ sprul pa dang ni rang brgyud kyi/ /man
5a7(rgyud 'grel): ngag rnams ni shes par bya/ /mdun du sprul dang bskyed pa ni/ /gtso bo'i dbang du bya ba dang/ /so so rang rang dbang du'o/ /de rnams cho ga la sogs kyang/ /man ngag bzhin du shes par bya'o/ /gnod sbyin kha dog dmar nag la/ /zhal gcig pa la phyag gnyis pa/ /
5b1(rgyud 'grel): g.yas g.yon gri gug cang te'u/ /ro langs ma ni sngo skya ste/ /zhal gcig pa la phyag gnyis pa/ /rdo rje lcags sgrog bzung nas ni/ /gung mo srin lag pa sogs rnams/ /dam por bkug pas yongs su bsdams/ /mtheb mdzub bzhi rnams rab brkyang ste/ /spyi bor nges par bsnol
5b2(rgyud 'grel): nas bsdams/ /rdo rje mkha' 'gro mdog ser skya/ /phyag gnyis spyi bor sbyar nas su/ /me lce'i phreng ba yongs su 'dzin/ /'jigs byed mdog ni sngo nag la/ /zhal gsum phyag drug zhabs gnyis pa/ /g.yas kyi dang po glang po rnams/ /g.yon pa glang po'i lpag pa bsnams/
5b3(rgyud 'grel): de 'og g.yas pa rdo rje bsnams/ /g.yon pa dgra sta bsnams pa'o/ /de 'og g.yas pa lcags kyu bsnams/ /g.yon pa mi mgo rlon pa bsnams/ /gnod sbyin mkha' 'gro de rnams kyang/ gtso bo gos sngon la bskor lha ne'i tshul/ /dkyil 'khor tshul gyi sgo thabs
5b4(rgyud 'grel): dang/ /yang na so so re re dang/ /rje khol tshul du gnas nas kyang/ /las rnams kun la mngag pa dang/ /yang na sbyor thabs tshul gnas nas/ /bsang mchod 'bul zhing phyag rgya bsgrub/ /gnod sbyin mkha' 'gro ma'i sbyor ka ste bdun pa'o// //rdo rje lha mo
5b5(rgyud 'grel): rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /lha mo 'di rnams cho ga yang/ /mkha' 'gro bzhin du 'dir shes bya/ /'od bskyed ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog dkar mo'o/ /phyag gnyis me tog bsnams pa'o/ /yid 'phrag ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ /sku mdog ser mo mdzes
5b6(rgyud 'grel): pa'i tshul/ /phyag gnyis dri yi spos por bsnams/ /kun bzang ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ /sku mdog dmar mo mdzes pa'i tshul/ /phyag gnyis zhal zas ro brgya ldan pa bsnams/ /klung sgra can ni zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ /sku mdog sngon mo mdzes pa'i tshul//
5b7(rgyud 'grel): phyag gnyis sgra brnyan gar gyis rol/ /lha mo 'di rnams kun la yang/ /dkyil 'khor las dang mchod pa'i tshul/ /gsum pa'i man ngag shes mod kyang/ /khyad par mchod pa'i tshul du bstan/ /mchod pa'i lha mo'i sbyor ka ste brgyad pa'o// //sgom bzhi la
6a1(rgyud 'grel): phyag 'tshal lo/ /sgo ma'i cho ga la sogs kyang/ /gong gi cho ga sbyor shes bya'o/ /srog gcod zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ /sku mdog mthing ga 'jigs pa'i tshul/ /phyag gnyis tho ba zhags pa bsnams/ /dbugs rdub ma zhal gcig
6a2(rgyud 'grel): phyag gnyis pa/ /sku mdog ser mo 'jigs pa'i tshul/ /phyag gnyis ho ma gzar zhags pa rnams/ /khrag 'thung ma zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ /sku mdog dmar mo 'jigs pa'i gzugs/ /phyag gnyis gri gug zhags pa bsnams/ /sha za ma
6a3(rgyud 'grel): zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ /sku mdog sngon mo 'jigs pa'i tshul/ /phyag gnyis snon po zhags pa bsnams/ /khro mo 'di rnams spyod tshul yang/ /dkyil 'khor las dang sbyor ba'i tshul/ /khyad par bsad pa'i las la shis/ /sgo ma bzhi'i sbyor ka ste dgu?
6a4(rgyud 'grel): pa'o// //bcom ldan rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnal 'byor blo rnams rim pa yis/ /bsdus rgya rim pa bstan par bya/ /pad+ma 'dab brgyad dkyil 'khor la/ /dbus dang 'dab brgyad lha dgu'o/ /phyi rim keng rus 'bar bas bskor/ /gru chang
6a5(rgyud 'grel): bzhi la lha mo bzhi po gnas/ /sgo rnams bzhi la sgo ma bzhi/ /'di ni rnal 'byor rgyas pa'i tshad/ /rnal 'byor bsdus la mos pa yis/ /lha ni bcu gsum bsgom par bya/ /de las kyang ni bsdus 'dod na/ /lha ni dgu po bsgom par bya/ /de las kyang ni bsdus
6a6(rgyud 'grel): 'dod na/ /lnga dang gsum dang gnyis dang gcig /man ngag cho ga mthong bas bya/ /ma mthong bas ni dam tshig nyams/ /de dag thams cad kun la yang/ /tshogs bsag lnga bskyed mkhas pas bya/ /bsdus rgya kyi sbyor ka ste bcu pa'o// //bcom ldan
6a7(rgyud 'grel): 'das rdo rje bsnams pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /lha rnams mchod pa'i rim pa ni/ /sha chen po las byung ba yi/ /dri mchog dud pa rgyun mi bcad/ /bde gshegs shangs la phul gyur pa/ /sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig /sha chen bdug spos dbul
6b1(rgyud 'grel): pa'o/ /b+ha ga rang byung me tog 'di/ /yid 'ong nam mkha' khyab tsam du/ /bde gshegs dbu la phul ba yis/ /sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig /rak+ta'i me tog dbul ba'o/ /tshil chen dur khrod ras las ni/ /ma rig mun sel sgron ma byung/ /bde gshegs spyan la phul gyur pas//
6b2(rgyud 'grel): sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig /tshil chen mar me dbul ba'o/ /mtshan dang ldan pa'i ka pA lar/ /rdo rje dri chus bkang nas su/ /bde gshegs thugs la phul gyur pas/ /sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig /rdo rje chu yis mchod pa'o/ /mtshan dang ldan pa'i ka pA la lar//
6b3(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje dri chen gtams nas su/ /bde gshegs ljags la phul gyur pas/ /sku gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig /dri chen lha bshos mchod pa'o/ /sil snyal rol mo dpag med rnams/ /yid 'ong mdzes par sprul nas su/ /bde gshegs snyan la phul gyur pas/ /sku
6b4(rgyud 'grel): gsung thugs mchog mnyes gyur cig /sgra dang rol mo'i mchod pa'o/ /rdo rje lha mo 'od bskyed ma/ /rdo rje me tog bsnams nas ni/ /mdzes pa'i tshul gyis mchod phul nas/ /mchod pa dam pa'i tshul gyis bzhes/ /rdo rje lha mo yid 'phrog ma/ /dri'i dung por bsnams nas su/ /gsang
6b5(rgyud 'grel): 'od? bzhad pa'i tshul gyis su/ /mchod pa dam pa dbul gyis bzhes/ /rdo rje lha mo kun bzang ma/ /zhal zas ro mchog bsnams nas su/ /dmar mo bzhad pa'i tshul gyis ni/ /mchod pa dam pa 'bul lo bzhes/ /rdo rje lha mo glu sgra can/ /sgra brnyan gar gyi rol mo yis//
6b6(rgyud 'grel): 'od sngon 'phros pa'i gzhad tshul gyis/ /mchod pa dam ba 'bul lo bzhes/ /sgeg mo la sogs brgyad rnams kyang/ /rgyud rnams gzhan dang mthun pas na/ /de bzhin 'dir yang dbul bar bya/ /rdo rje glu rnams mdzes pa yis/ /bstun nas lha la mchod pa 'bul/ /mchod pa'i
6b7(rgyud 'grel): sbyor ka ste bcu gcig pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /lha rnams bstod pa'i rim pa ni/ /bcom ldan rdo rje gos sngon can/ /sku mdog sngon po 'jigs pa'i tshul/ /rdo rje stobs kyis 'byung po 'dul/ /rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/
7a1(rgyud 'grel): rnam rgyal rdo rje khro bo ni/ /dbu gsum phyag drug 'jigs pa'i gzugs/ /sku mdog 'od dmar bgegs rnams bsreg /bdud las rgyal la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /dpal ldan mgon po nag po ni/ /nag po'i zhags pa 'dzin ma? cing/ /tsan dan bed kyis? thams
7a2(rgyud 'grel): cad 'joms/ /mthu chen khyod la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /lus ngan po ni rgyal po'i mchog /mchod pa'i rten gyis don rnams 'grub/ /ne'u le rin chen gter brtan rnams/ /dgos 'dod bskod la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /khro bo bdud rtsis bdud rnams 'joms/ /phyag rgya sdig
7a3(rgyud 'grel): mdzub mdzad pa yis/ /sdang mig mi 'gyur zhe la gnon/ /'od sngon po la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /gnod sbyin khro bo 'jigs pa'i gzugs/ /sku mdog dmar nag 'od zer can/ /gri gug 'bar bas gcod mdzad ma/ /cang te'u sgrogs la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /ro langs ma ni mthu mo che
7a4(rgyud 'grel): po? skya rdo rje lcags sgrog sdom/ /phyag rgya spyi bor bsnol mdzad ma/ /ro langs ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /rdo rje mkha' 'gro dpal 'bar ma/ /dmar skya me lce phreng ba 'dzin/ /rdo rje mes ni thams cad bsreg /rdo rje mkha' 'gro phyag 'tshal bstod/ /'jig byed ma ni thams cad
7a5(rgyud 'grel): 'joms/ /sngo nag zhal gsum phyag drug pa/ /phyag mtshan drug gis 'byung po 'dul/ /'jigs byed ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /rdo rje lha mo 'od bskyed ma/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog dkar/ /rdo rje me tog phyag na bsnams/ /'od bskyed ma la phyag 'tshal
7a6(rgyud 'grel): bstod/ /rdo rje lha mo yid 'phrog ma/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog ser/ /dri mchog dpag med phyag na bsnams/ /yid 'phrog ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /rdo rje lha mo kun bzangs ma/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog dmar/ /zhal zas ro mchog brgya ldan bsnams
7a7(rgyud 'grel): kun bzang ma la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /rdo rje lha mo glu sgra can/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog sngo/ /sgra brnyan gar gyi rol pas gnas/ /glu sgra can la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /rdo rje khro mo srog gcod ma/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog gnag /sgrub la gnod pa'i
7b1(rgyud 'grel): srog gcod ma/ /tho ba zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /khro mo rdo rje dbugs rdub ma/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog ser/ /sgrub la gnod pa'i dbugs rdub ma/ /hoM gzar zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /khro mo chen mo khrag 'thung ma/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis
7b2(rgyud 'grel): sku mdog dmar/ /sgrub la gnod pa'i khrag 'thung ma/ /gri gug zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /khro mo chen mo sha za ma/ /zhal gcig phyag gnyis sku mdog sngo/ /sgrub la gnod pa'i sha za ma/ /rnon po zhags pa bsnams la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /rdo rje glu ni mdzes
7b3(rgyud 'grel): pa yis/ /bstod pa rnams kyis lha bstod pas/ /tshogs chen dpag med sogs par 'gyur/ /bstod pa'i sbyor ka ste bcu gnyis pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal te/ /rdor dril byin brlabs mchod pa bstan/ /rdor dril rab gnas byas pa dang
7b4(rgyud 'grel): dang po stong dang snying rje las/ /yi ge a hUM rnam gnyis phyung/ /de las rdor dril bskyed par bya/ /ye shes rdor dril byin brlabs bstim/ /yang na rab gnas byas pa la/ /dang po byin brlabs gsal bas chog /lag na rdo rje byin brlabs la/ /lag mthil nyi zla ba
7b5(rgyud 'grel): byin gyis brlab/ /lag g.yon mthe bong srin lag gis/ /rdo rje dril bu blang bar bya/ /dril bu 'og la rdo rje steng/ /brla g.yon steng du bzhag par bya/ /lag g.yas srin lag mthe bong gis/ /rdo rje ra brag btsugs nas ni/ /bskor ba'i tshul gyis thugs khar blang
7b6(rgyud 'grel): rgyu yi yi ge gnyis po yang/ /rdor dril la ni mtshan mar bsam/ phyag na rdo rje'i ting 'dzin gyis/ /'gying bag tshul gyis bstan par bya/ /dang po g.yon du gar gsum bsgyur/ /de nas g.yas su gar gsum bsgyur/ /de nas thugs ka mgrin pa dang/ /spyi bo dag tu gar
7b7(rgyud 'grel): gsum bsgyur/ /de nas slar la phab nas ni/ /lte ba la sogs gnas brgyad du/ /rdo rje dril gnyis gsor bar bya/ /de nas dril bu lan gsum dang/ /rdo rje lan gsum gsor bar bya/ /de nas rdo rje dril thabs ni/ /brgyad kyi tshul du mchod par bya/ dang po rdo rje
8a1(rgyud 'grel): dril du gnyis/ /gsor zhing thugs kar brtan par gzung/ /de nas rdo rje dril bu gnyis/ /bsnol zhing 'khyud nas mchod pa 'bul/ /de nas rdo rje dril bu gnyis/ /nu ma g.yas g.yon thad ka ru/ /rdo rje steng la dril bu 'og /bsnol zhing 'gying bag
8a2(rgyud 'grel): phan tshun bkyer/ /de nas rdo rje dril bu gnyis/ /gar gyi tshul du bstod nas kyang/ /rdor dril lan gnyis gsor bar bya/ /dril bu thugs ka'i thad kar gsil/ /rdo rje dpung g.yon thang gsor nas/ /da nas sa la bkyer bar bya/ /slar la log cing dpung g.yon bskor/
8a3(rgyud 'grel): dril bu thugs kar thad bsil la/ /rdo rje gsor nas thugs kar ni/ /thad kar dkrol zhing gzung bar bya/ /rdo rje dang ni dril bu gnyis/ /gar gyi tshul du bkyer ba dang/ /rdo rje dang ni dril bu gnyis/ /g.yas g.yon dbang du bkyer ba dang/ /de ltar rdo rje dril thabs
8a4(rgyud 'grel): kyis/ /rdo rje glu dang bstun nas su/ /bde gshegs rnams la mchod pa 'bul/ /glu gar rtsed 'jo'i phyag rgya yis/ /'dzul lam nam mkhar 'phur bar 'gyur/ /rnal 'byor tshogs 'khor tshogs mchod kyi/ /spros la dga' ba'i dus su bya/ /rnal 'byor bsdus pa 'dod 
8a5(rgyud 'grel): pa yis/ /sbyor thabs tshul gyi bzhi po bya/ /shin tu bsdus pa 'dod pa yis/ /lha rnams bstod pa bar bar du/ /rdo rje dril thabs gsor bar bya/ /yang na dril bu rgyun du la/ /rdo rje mtshams su shes par bya/ /de rnams bsam pa'i mchod pa yang/ /yi ge gnyis kyi man
8a6(rgyud 'grel): ngag gam/ /thabs dang shes rab mchod pa 'am/ /phyag 'tshal tshul du bya ba'o/ /rdo rje dril thabs kyi sbyor ka ste bcu gsum pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /phyag rgya'i rim pa bstan pa ni/ /g.yas kyi gung mo dag la ni//
8a7(rgyud 'grel): sor mo bzhi po btsugs nas kyang/ /rtse lnga'i tshul du bya ba dang/ /g.yon pa'i sor mo spro ba 'am/ /sgra sgrogs tshul du byed pa'am/ /yang na mthe bong mthe chung gnyis/ /bkug nas gsum po rtse gsum tshul/ /g.yas pa snga ma dang 'dra la/ /g.yon pa'i gung mo
8b1(rgyud 'grel): bkug nas su/ /mdzub mo rgyab sbyar bkug pa'o/ /sor mo rnams kyang bcings nas su/ /gung mo mthe bong ngos btung nas/ /gzhan rnams yongs su brkyang ba yis/ /lag g.yas mtheb 'dzub zhags pa bya/ /g.yon gyi mtheb mdzub ral gri'i tshul/ /gnyis ka lhag ma
8b2(rgyud 'grel): rnams ni bcing/ /g.yas kyi khu tshur bcings nas su/ /mthe bong nang nas gdon bar bya/ /g.yon gyi mthe bor mdzub mor sbyar/ lhag ma rnams ni bcing bar bya/ /lag gnyis rdo rje thal mo las/ /gung mo la ni mdzub mo sbyar/ /mthe bong bsnol te sbyar bar bya/ /yang
8b3(rgyud 'grel): na lag gnyis sbyar ba 'am/ /g.yon gyi sor mo sbyar? bsdus pa'o/ /lag gnyis khu tshur bcangs nas ni/ /mdzub mo spreng te brang du bsnol/ /g.yas kyi khu tshur bcangs nas ni/ /mdzub mo dang ni gung mo dgug /g.yon gyi khu tshur bcangs te bskor/ gung srin la sogs
8b4(rgyud 'grel): gsum pa rnams/ /dam por bkug nas yongs su bsam/? /mtheb mdzub bzhi rnams rab brkyang ste/ /spyi bor nges par bsnol nas gnas/ /phyag gnyis spyi bor thal sbyar nas/ /me lce phreng ba yongs su 'dzin/ /lag pa g.yas g.yon 'dzin tshul dang/ /g.yas pa khu tshur
8b5(rgyud 'grel): bcangs nas ni/ /gung mo bkug pa'i rgyab tu ni/ /mdzub mo nges par sbyar bar bya/ /mdzub mo lcags kyu'i tshul dang ni/ /g.yon gyi sor mo bsdus te bskor/ /lag gnyis mtheb mdzub sbyar nas ni/ /gsum po brkyang ste rtse mor sbyar/ /lag g.yas khu tshur bcangs nas ni//
8b6(rgyud 'grel): gung mo brkyang ste g.yon pa yi/ /khu tshur bcangs te gru mo gzugs/ /lag pa sbyar te bskongs pa dang/ /sgra snyan gar gyi rol pas gnas/ /lag g.yas khu chur tho ba'i tshul/ /g.yon pa mtheb mdzub zhags pa'i tshul/ /lag g.yas sor mo bskongs pa dang/ /g.yon
8b7(rgyud 'grel): pa mtheb mdzub sbyar te bcang/ /lag g.yas gung mo srin lag gnyis/ /bkug ste gsum pa bcing bar bya/ /lag g.yon mtheb mdzub sbyar te bcang/ /g.yas kyi gung mo mdzub mo brkyang/ /srin lag mthe chung mthe bos mnan/ /g.yon gyi mtheb mdzub
9a1(rgyud 'grel): sbyar te bcad/ /phyag rgya'i sbyor ka ste bcu bzhi pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/ /oM nI lAm+ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni huM hUM phaT/ oM trai lo kya bi dza ya hUM phaT/ oM mahA yak+Sha se nA pa tA ye/ nI lAm+ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA
9a2(rgyud 'grel): Ni hUM hUM hUM/ phaT phaT phaT/ oM badzra yak+Sha hUM phaT/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra mahA yak+Sha se nA pa ha ye badzra pA Ni hUM hUM phaT swAhA/ oM mahA kA la ro Sha Na hUM phaT/ oM bai sh+ra ma Ni hUM phaT/ oM nI lAm+ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni mahA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye hUM phaT/ oM pra bi da pa ta ye hUM phaT/ oM
9a3(rgyud 'grel): ? me me ha ra ya hUM phaT/ oM a mri ta kuN+Da li ha na ha na hUM phaT/ oM sa man+ta bag tri ya hUM phaT/ oM shapda gI b+ha ya hUM phaT/ oM badzra pe ta li hUM phaT/ oM pra taM sta na ya hUM phaT/ oM sha mo gu pa ya hUM phaT/ oM ra ga d+ha pri ya ni hUM phaT/ oM badzra rA ki ya hUM phaT/ oM
9a4(rgyud 'grel): man sa ba k+Shi ni hUM phaT/ oM badzra be ra ya hUM phaT/ oM rak+ta ka ra lo ka bi sha na/ ni lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni ya/ na gwa la ga ra ba ta ke twa byAg+h+ra tsar ma Ni ba sa ni ya b+ha ma ko re ga ru ra ru sti ma ti maM/ kro d+ha mArte na trai lo kya h+ra ha ya/ bruM me na ko pa yas na ru tra ya nA ga  
9a5(rgyud 'grel): ? tur ma ra b+hak+Sha ya hUM phaT/ oM trai lo kya bi dza ya hUM phaT/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni maN+Da la de ba ta naM/ puShpa pU dza me g+ha sa mu dra spha ra Na sa ma ye hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni/ maN+Da la da ba pa ta naM/ d+hU pa pU dza me g+ha sa mu dra spha ra Na sa ma ye hUM/
9a6(rgyud 'grel): oM nI lAM ba da d+ha ra badzra pA Ni/ maN+Dal de ba tA nAM/ A lo ke pU dza me g+ha sa mu dra spha ra Na sa ma ye hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni/ maN+Dal de ba ta naM/ gand+he pU dza me g+ha sa mu dra spha ra Na sa ma ye hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA ni/ /maN+Dal de ba ta naM/ nai bi dye pU dza
9a7(rgyud 'grel): me g+ha sa mu dra spha ra Na sa ma ye hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA ni/ maN+Dal de ba ta naM/ shapta pU dza me g+ha sa mu dra spha ra Na sa ma ye hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA ni/ maN+Da la de ba ta naM/ tsa ri pU dza me g+ha sa mu dra spha ra Na sa ma ye hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA
9b1(rgyud 'grel): ni maN+Da la de ba ta naM/ ta ri nIrya ta yA mi hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni/ maN+Da la de ba te naM/ bastra nirya ta yA mi hUM/ oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni/ maN+Da la de ba ta naM/ gar dar ba nIrya ta yA mi hUM/ oM nI lAm+ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni/ maN+Da la de ba ta naM/ ma Ni ratna sarba bstu nirya
9b2(rgyud 'grel): ta yA mi hUM/ oM nI lAm+ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni/ maN+Da la de ba ta naM/ parshe nIrya ta yA mi hUM/ oM tsa Na mahA ro Sha Na Arya a' rya si d+ha ya hUM phaT swAhA/ oM ma Ni d+ha ri badzra pA Ni hUM phaT swAhA/ oM bastu ratna ba hi hUM phaT/ oM a mri ti si ti hUM phaT/ oM saM ma shi ta ya ba ra ba hUM
9b3(rgyud 'grel): phaT?/ oM ?? sha sa pa ra hUM phaT/ oM ku mA ri b+ha dza sha ma ni hUM phaT/ oM badzra pA ni hUM phaT/ oM badzra pA Ni hUM hUM/ tadya thA/ b+ha b+ha pa ni nA ga a d+hi pa ta ye/ aM di nA lAm+ba ra d+ha ra sha rI raM badzra pA Ni/ h+ri da yaM ya(rgyud 'grel): sa mA ti kra ma tha mA ku la ?? naM/ b+ha pi ? ti/ tadya thA/
9b4(rgyud 'grel): bud+d+ha sarb+ha?/ bi bud+d+ha/ bi bud+d+ha/ mA ti kra ma tha/ ha ra ha ra nA gA nAM/ pra ha ra pra ha ra nA gA nAM/ tshinda tshinda/ nA ga h+ri da yA ni/ b+hinda b+hinda/ nA ga marma Ni bi sh'ryan+tu/ nA ga sha rI rA Ni/ bi spho Ta ya/ nA ga nA ya nA ni/ tadya thA/ hUM phaT/ nA ga bi dA ra? ? hUM phaT/ nA ga ut+ma danda
9b5(rgyud 'grel): ya hUM phaT/ nI lAM ba sa nA ya hUM phaT/ a pra ti ha ha pa la pa ra kra mA ya phaT/ gri bAn+ta ya phaT/ kri hAn+ta rU pA ya phaT/ ro Sha NA ya phaT/ trA sa nA ya phaT/ ku b+hAM Do tas dA nA ya phaT/ pri ta pi shA tsi bi nA sha ka rA ya phaT/ yak+Sha a pa sma ra pi nA sha ka rA ya phaT/
9b6(rgyud 'grel): ha sa ha sa/ d+ha ra d+ha ra/ mA ra ya mA ra ya/ nA sha ya nA sha ya/ sarba big+h+nAM /bi nA sha kaM rA ya phaT/ sarba sha truM saM g+ha bi nA sha ka rA ya phaT/ nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni rA dz+nyA pa ya ti swAhA/ /sngags kyi sbyor ba'i rim pa yang/ /bsnyen dang bsgrub pa las kyi sbyor
9b7(rgyud 'grel): ba'i sngags kyi rim par bya'o/ /dbye ba'i rim pa ma shes na/ /las rnams 'grub par mi 'gyur ro/ /de brtson slob dpon la gus pas/ /ser sna g.yo rgyu med pas su/ /yon gyis bla ma mnyes byas la/ /yang yang mnyan pas man ngag ni/ /the tshom med pa
10a1(rgyud 'grel): shin tu gces/ /de bas man ngag can ni btsal/ /man ngag med pa'i nan rtags la/ /dngos grub thob par mi 'gyur ro/ /sngags kyi sbyor ka ste bco lnga pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sngags rnams kyi ni btung ba'i
10a2(rgyud 'grel): mchog /byas pas the tshom sel bar 'gyur/ /phyag 'tshal mgo la brgyan par bya/ /kA li'i sde tshan bzhi pa yi/ /bzhi ba dag la is su brgyan/ /kA li'i sde tshan drug pa yi/ /gsum pa dag la mas su brgyan/ /ba zhes bya ba yi ge la/ /ha zhes bya ba'i yi ge btabs/ /de 'og ra
10a3(rgyud 'grel): yi yi ge'o/ /da la ha btags de 'og ra/ /de 'og ba dang dza la ni/ /ra btags pa ni de yi 'og /na la is brgyan hUM dang phaT/ /yang na hUM gnyis sogs pa'am/ /yi ge bcu gsum pa zhes bya/ /cho ga par mchod pa'i dbang du byas/ /oM gyi yi ge dang por mtshan/ /yi ge na la
10a4(rgyud 'grel): dbyings? su brgyan/ /yi ge la la mas su brgyan/ /ba la ta ni btags par bya/ /ra yi yi ge gcig phug nas/ /da la ha ni gdags par bya/ /ra yi yi ge gcig pu gnas/ /ba dang dza ni sdebs pa la/ /yi ge ra ni gdags par bya/ ba ni gcig pu gnas pa la/ /na la is su brgyan
10a5(rgyud 'grel): par bya/ /ma dang ha dang ya dang gsum/ /gdags pa med de so sor gnas/ /ka la sha ni gdags par bya/ /sa la es su brgyan par bya/ /na dang pa dang ta dang gsum/ /gdags pa med de lugs su gnas/ /ya la es su brgyan par bya/ /ha la u ni btags nas su/ /zla
10a6(rgyud 'grel): tshes thig les brgyan par bya/ /pha ni gcig pu ta ni bzlog/ yang na hUM gsum phaT kyang gsum/ /hUM gnyis dang ni phaT gnyis ni/ /las gzhan drag po'i skabs dang sbyar/ /man ngag can gyis shes par bya/ /yi ge nyi shu rtsa gcig ces/ /chog par bcad par shes
10a7(rgyud 'grel): par bya/ /yang na hUM gnyis bsnan pa rtsa gnyis pa/ /ya yi yi ge drag po gnyis/ /bsnan pas rtsa bzhi pa zhes bya/ /de yang drag po'i skabs yin pas/ /khyad par du ni shes par bya/ /yi ge rkang grangs dbang byas na/ /de ltar ma nges rtsa drug nas/ /sum cu rtsa gcig bar du
10b1(rgyud 'grel): yod/ /oM gyi yi ge dang por mtshan/ /mtshan gyi yi ge'i steng du ni/ /ma dang ha dang tsha dang na dang ni/ /da la ha ni !gdags par bya/ /ra la os su brgyan pa ni/ /sha dang na dang ha la u/ /zla tshes thig le ta la brgyan/ /pha dang ta log yi ge'o/ /yi ge bcu gsum zhes su bya//
10b2(rgyud 'grel): yi ge drug ces bya ba ni/ /mtshan gyi man ngag kho na'o/ /swAhA/ oM dang ho dang gsum/ /zhi rgyas dbang gi yi ge mdza' / /dza sogs pa yi yi ge rnams/ /'gug pa la sogs mdza' ru bstan/ /man ngag can gyis sbyor zhes bya'o/ /yi ge hUM ni 'bru gcig po/ /'di
10b3(rgyud 'grel): yang bzlas pa'i yi ge snying po yin/ /yi ge btu ba ma shes na/ /sngags kyi mthu ni nyams par 'gyur/ /de bas nan tan bskyed de btu/ /lha rnams gzhan po'i sngags rnams kyang/ /bdag gi btu ba ma nus pas/ /slob dpon la ni gus bya'i phyir/ /slob dpon rna
10b4(rgyud 'grel): rgyur man ngag las/ /yi ge btu ba shes par bya/ /yi ge btu ba'i sbyor ka ste bcu drug pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bzlas brjod man ngag bstan par bya/ /phyi dang nang dang gsang ba dang/ /bla med bzlas brjod bzhi ru bstan/ /dang po phyi
10b5(rgyud 'grel): yi bzlas pa ni/ /sems dpa' sum rtseg tshul du bya/ /de ni kun gyi thun mong yin/ /khyad par re re 'am gnyis sdebs su/ /las kyi khyad par skabs dang sbyar/ /mtshon gar nas dang rta rnga'i tshul/ /mtshon gyi sum cha de yi phyad/ /pad+ma la sogs mtshon gyi phyed/ /rin
10b6(rgyud 'grel): chen rmug po gur lta bu/ /dad pa'i rgyu yi tshad tsam mo/ /yang na dar mo gru gsum ni/ /tsi ta'i tshad tsam nyid du 'dod/ /de lta'i gnas ni nyid du yang/ /ye shes bzhugs pa'i gnas su 'dod/ /la la dag gi bzhed kyis ni/ /rang byung nyid du yod par 'dod/ /de ni rgyu 'am nus pa'i tshul
10b7(rgyud 'grel): la la dag gi bzhed kyis ni/ /de nyid las ni sprul pa yi/ /kun brtags de la de skad gdags/ /gzhan yang gzhung lugs mi mthun pa'i/ /dang po dbang bskur dus su ni/ /dang por dkyil 'khor bcug pa'i lha dang ni/ /de nyid so so tha dad 'dod/ /thugs ka dbu steng gong
11a1(rgyud 'grel): 'og gnas/ /lha nyid 'jug pa'i tshul la yang/ /'khor lo rdzogs pa'am lha de nyid/ /bdag nyid man ngag thob gzhung gis/ /lha de rkyen gyi tshul yin la/ /rang 'byung nus pa rgyu yin pas/ /gnyis med gcig tu bsdebs te bsgom/ /de ltar the tshom
11a2(rgyud 'grel): bcad nas ni/ rang gi rig pa pho brang nyid/ /shin tu gsal bar sbyangs nas ni/ mi shes lha la bsnyen pa 'bul/ /dang po 'od zer spros nas ni/ /ye shes spyan drangs lha de la/ /mtshan ma la sogs gsal nas ni/ /'khor lo bzhin du dbul ba dang/ /pad+ma brtsegs dang rin chen
11a3(rgyud 'grel): thag de nyid thun mong shes par bya'o/ /lugs 'byung lugs bzlog 'khor lo'i tshul/ /shes rab sbyor thabs mchod pa'i tshul/ /mchog gi dngos grub 'dod pa'o/ /lce ni rdo rje dkar por bsgyur/ /yang na sngo ljang nyid du bya/ /nyi ma shar ba bzhin du gdal/ /de ni sngon du nyams
11a4(rgyud 'grel): pa'i tshul/ drag po bsgrub pa'i gnas skabs su/ /man ngag gong bzhin bzlog ste gsal/ /lce ni rdo rje ser po dang/ /dmar po rgyas dang dbang la shis/ /mthing ka drag po'i tshul du bstan/ /'od zer 'khor lugs gong bzhin no/ /las kyi rim pa'i
11a5(rgyud 'grel): skabs dang sbyar/ /ba thag tsha tsha'i tshul dang ni/ /drag po kho na'i skabs dang sbyar/ /rul chu brug ba bzhin du 'am/ /srin po dur skad ji bzhin du/ /shin tu drag cing myur bar bzlas/ /las kyi khyad par gzhan dag la/ /spros te sbyangs pa'i tshul dang ni/
11a6(rgyud 'grel): 'od zer spu gu btsugs pa dang/ /me yi tshul gyis bsregs pa dang/ /lcags kyu lta bus bkug pa dang/ /mtshon cha char bzhin dbab pa dang/ /'khor lo bzhin du bskor ba dang/ /mnan pa'i tshul du bya ba dang/ /mnga' zam tshul du bya ba dang/ 'khrul
11a7(rgyud 'grel): 'khor tshul du bya ba dang/ /'phen sdud tshul du bya ba dang/ /dang pos bkug la gnyis pas bsreg /dang pos bkug la gnyis pas bsad/ /dang pos bkug la gnyis bas mnan/ /yang na gsum sdebs tshul gyis bya/ /bzhi ba sdebs lnga
11b1(rgyud 'grel): bsdebs pa yang yin/ /bsdebs sbyor cho ga thams cad kyang/ /man ngag bzhin du shes par bya/ /de la sogs pa'i man ngag rnams/ /brgyud pa las ni shes bar bya'o/ /de rnams bzlas brjod byed pa yang/ /sems ni gzhan du mi g.yeng zhing/ /tshig
11b2(rgyud 'grel): gzhan gyis ni bar mi chor/ /yi ge man ngag ma nyams par/ /sgra yi brjod tshul skabs dang sbyar/ /de la nan tan tshar bskyed la/ /mtshan ma'i dngos grub 'byung bar 'gyur/ /mtshan ma'i dngos grub gsum po yang/ /dang por ba la gsum du
11b3(rgyud 'grel): bstan/ /sprul dang yang sprul sum sprul lo/ /'bring la sgra dang dri dang ni/ /'od du yang ni bstan pa yin/ /tha ma nam smad nam stong dang/ /nyin mo dag dang gsum du bstan/ /de dag rtags rnams kun la yang/ /gzugs ni sdug dang mi sdug dang/
11b4(rgyud 'grel): drin zhim dang mi zhim dang/ /sgra ni snyan dang mi snyan dang/ /ro yang zhim dang mi zhim dang/ /'od dkar 'od ser 'od dmar po/ /ljang dang nag la sogs pa yi/ /rtags la sogs pa de dag la/ /gsum dang bdun dang bco lnga dang/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig
11b5(rgyud 'grel): zhag du brtag /thams cad brtan zhing mi 'gyur dang/ /phung po khams gsal ting 'dzin gsal/ /'dod la sogs pa zhi ba'i tshul/ /de sogs rtags rnams byung ba na/ /lha yi dngos grub yin par brtag /mtshan ma la sogs mi brtan zhing/ /
11b6(rgyud 'grel): phung po la sogs myos 'gyur zhing/ /ting 'dzin rnams ni mi gsal ba/ /'od dmar gnag cing rtsub 'gyur na/ /de la sogs pa'i rtags rnams kyang/ /bdud kyi rtags su shes par bya/ /rtags rnams de rnams byung na yang/ /don dam rang
11b7(rgyud 'grel): bzhin med pa la/ /kun rdzob sgyu ma lta bu'i sems/ /re dang dogs pa rnams spangs te/ /dga' dang mi dga' i sems mi bya/ /'jigs pa la sogs sems spang ste/ /maN+Dal me tog bcas phul nas/ /sbyin sreg 'khor lo la sogs bya/ /de ltar byas
12a1(rgyud 'grel): tshe mkha' 'gro mas/ /lung bstan gnas su khrid pa dang/ /man ngag 'jigs pa med pas blang/ /bdud kyi ltas rnams 'byung ba ni/ /gong bzhin byas pas med par 'gyur/ /nang na mtshan ma bsnyen pa
12a2(rgyud 'grel): gtso/ /de 'og grangs kyi bsnyen pa gtso/ /dus kyi bsnyen pa tha ma'o/ /grangs kyi rab 'bring tha ma ni/ /gtso po 'bum dang nyis 'bum dang/ /sum 'bum dag tu shes par bya/ /rnam rgyal la sogs bzhi po la/ /'bum phyir 'bum
12a3(rgyud 'grel): dang nyi 'bum mo/ /'khor rnams lhag ma kun la ni/ /khri dang nyi khri sum khri'o/ /yang na lha rnams so so yi/ /sku gcig bsnyen la byed pa ni/ /rab kyi bsnyen pa sum 'bum mo/ /'bring gi bsnyen pa bdun 'bum mo/ /tha
12a4(rgyud 'grel): ma'i bsnyen pa bye ba'o/ /dus la yang ni gsum gsum yong/ /zla gcig zla gnyis zla gsum bar/ lo phyed zla dgu lo gcig gi /lo gnyis dang ni lo gsum dang/ /lo bzhi tha mar shes par bya/ /de ltar byas kyang ma byung
12a5(rgyud 'grel): na/ /dam tshig nyams pa yin pas na/ /sbyin sreg tshogs 'khor la sogs kyis/ /dam tshig nyams pa bskang nas ni/ /slar la sogs pa'i cho ga bya/ /de ltar byas kyang ma byung na/ /rnal 'byor sdig sgrib che bas na/ /sbyin
12a6(rgyud 'grel): sreg tshogs 'khor la sogs kyis/ /sdig sgrib la sogs sbyangs nas ni/ /slar la sogs pa'i cho ga bya/ /de ltar byas kyang ma byung na/ /yang na bsgom pa gcig pus bya/ /yang na bzlas brjod gcig pus so/ /bsgom dang
12a7(rgyud 'grel): bzlas pa'i dngos grub ni/ /'byung bar de ni ma gyur na/ /tshogs 'khor tshogs mchod sbyin sreg dang/ /gtor ma la sogs so so la/ /man ngag cho ga thob pas na/ /dngos grub nges par 'byung bar 'gyur/ /de dag thams cad
12b1(rgyud 'grel): kun la yang/ /the tshom can gyis mi 'grub ste/ /the tshom med nges 'grub par 'gyur/ /de ltar byas kyang ma byung na/ /mtshan ma gsum mam nus pa brtag /yungs kar dag la sngags bzlas nas/ /shing ljon la sogs me tog la/ /btab
12b2(rgyud 'grel): nas bskams 'gyur rab yin no/ /chu la bzlas te gtor ba na/ /char pa la sogs 'bebs pa dang/ /thal ba la ni sngags bzlas na/ /char pa la sogs gcod par 'gyur/ /da ni 'bring gi nus pa brtag /yungs kar phyag mtshan
12b3(rgyud 'grel): la sogs pas/ /sngags bzlas gtor zhing brabs pa yis/ /gdon dang nang la sogs pa sel/ /de ni tha ma'i nus pa'i rtags/ /de ltar byas kyang ma byung na/ /lha sogs man ngag thams cad spro/ /khams dang bag chags med
12b4(rgyud 'grel): phyir ro/ /cho ga thams cad gong bzhin no/ /man ngag mi mthun gzhan yang sbyar/ /de ltar byas na dngos grub 'byung/ /dngos grub byung bar ma gyur kyang/ /sgrib pa rnams ni mgo mnan nas/ tshogs chen khyad par bsags nas ni/ /daM tshig ma nyams
12b5(rgyud 'grel): rnal 'byor pas/ /skye ba phyi ma la sogs su/ /dngos grub rnams ni thob par 'gyur/ /dngos grub khyad par ma thob na/ /skye ba bdun la gdon mi za/ /nang gi bzlas brjod bstan pa ni/ /rnal 'byor lam pa rnams kyis ni/ /snying ka'i 'khor
12b6(rgyud 'grel): lo la sogs la/ /rang 'byung yi ge nus pa ni/ /rlung gi rta la zhon nas kyang/ /snying ka'i 'khor lo la sogs bskor/ /gsang ba'i bzlas brjod man ngag ni/ /byang chub sems kyi man ngag gam/ /phyag rgya la brten ji bzhin
12b7(rgyud 'grel): no/ /mthar thug gi ni bzlas pa yang/ /snang ba gsum gyi mdza' la ni/ /mi rtog ye shes stong nyid gsal/ /de ni bzlas pa'i mchog yin no/ /bzlas pa'i rim pa'i man ngag ni/ /rnal 'byor blo dman don du bstan/ /
13a1(rgyud 'grel): bzlas brjod kyi man ngag gi sbyor ka ste bcu bdun pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rdzogs rim man ngag cung zhig bstan/ /
13a2(rgyud 'grel): dngos po gnas pa'i gnas lugs dang/ /blos su bsams pa'i rim pa yi/ /dngos po gnas pa'i gnas lugs ngag la yang/ /rtsa dang rlung dang byang chub sems/ /rtsa yi gtso bo d+hU tI yin/ /d+hU tI nyid kyi
13a3(rgyud 'grel): gzhung lugs kyang/ /srog rtsa nang du rgyu ba dang/ /de la brten par 'dod pa'o/ /de la sogs pa'i gzhung lugs mang/ /bdag gi gzhung gis nang du rgyu/ /shin tu phra ba rta rnga tshad/ /de bas phra bar
13a4(rgyud 'grel): 'dod pa'ang yod/ /dbugs kyi dangs ma shin tu phra/ /'od dang ldan pa nyid la ni/ /byang chub sems ni til mar bzhin/ /de la khyab par brten pa yi/ /g.yas dang g.yon gyi rtsa gnyis ni/ /la la nA
13a5(rgyud 'grel): dang ra sa nA/ /mdun gyi rtsa ni da da dz+nyA/ /de rnams tshad la sogs pa yang/ /d+hU tI nyid dang mthun pa'o/ /rtsa yi 'khor lo rnams la yang/ /gzhung lugs mi 'dra mang du bstan/ /'khor lo gcig dang
13a6(rgyud 'grel): 'khor lo gnyis/ /'khor lo bzhi dang 'khor lo drug /'khor lo brgyad dang 'khor lo dgu /rdo rje nor bu'i cha la yang/ /pho brang bzhi yi gnas ngag tu/ /'khor lo mi mthun 'dod pa dang/ /
13a7(rgyud 'grel): 'khor lo mang po 'dod pa rnams/ /in+d+ra bo d+hi gzhung lugs yin/ /rlung gi gzhung lugs dag la yang/ /lte ba'i lkog dang lte ba dang/ /snying gar mgrin pa yan lag gi /gnas ni lnga po dag
13b1(rgyud 'grel): las kyang/ /srog gi rlung dang gyen du rgyu/ /me dang mnyam nas thur du sel/ /kun la khyab pa'i rlung rnams ni/ /gnas lnga tha dad gtso bo yin/ /yan lag lnga dang dbang po lnga/ /de ltar tha dad 'dod pa'ang yod/
13b2(rgyud 'grel): bdag gi gzhung gi gnas skabs kyis/ /las kyi sgo nas phye bas na/ /thams cad ngo bo gcig yin no/ /byang sems 'bebs pa'i gtum mo yang/ /'khor lo rten dang mi brten pa'i/ /drag 'dzin ma ni bcu bzhi po/ /
13b3(rgyud 'grel): in+d+ra bo d+hi la sogs gzhung/ /rang bzhin gtum mo 'dod par ni/ /mkhas pa rnams ni kun ka mthun/ /byang chub sems la gnyis yod do/ /don dam dang ni kun rdzob bo/ /kun rdzob la yang gnyis yod de/ /
13b4(rgyud 'grel): snyigs mar gyur dang bcud du gyur/ /bcud du gyur la gnyis yod de/ /til mar bzhin du khyab pa dang/ /'chi ba'i dus tshe 'byung ba'o/ /de la brten pa'i man ngag tshogs/ /rim pa bzhin du shes par bya'o/ /bsam
13b5(rgyud 'grel): zhing bsgom pa'i rim pa yang/ /rang 'byung yi ge'i gnas tshul ni/ /yi ge hUM dang a dang ni/ /oM dang haM gi rnam pa bzhi/ /man ngag sbyor rdzogs shes par bya/ /'khor lo rnams ni gsal byas la/ /lte bar
13b6(rgyud 'grel): /gtum mo zhes bya lte ba'i lkog /sor gnyis sor bzhi sor drug /mgrin pa A li bcu drug go /dung khang la ni nyis ldab bo/ /gtum mo zhes bya lte ba'i lkog /sor gnyis sor bzhi sor drug tu/ /mar me bzhin
13b7(rgyud 'grel): du gnas pa las/ /rlung la nyi ma'i stobs kyis su/ /las kyi rlung ni sngon mo bcus/ /spar nas de la gtad par bya/ /rtags brgyad byung nas shin tu spar/ /dga' ba la sogs rim skyes pas/ /rtags lnga'i
14a1(rgyud 'grel): mthar ni stong par 'gyur/ /'khor lo gcig dang 'khor lo gnyis/ /gsum la sogs pa'i man ngag ni/ /rim pa bzhin du sbyor shes bya'o/ /rlung rnams g.yas dang g.yon du ni/ /gnyi
14a2(rgyud 'grel): kar rgyu dang ngal bar rgyu/ /de la gtad pa'i rim gyis ni/ /spro bar nus na bsdu bar bya'o/ /rtags lnga'i mthar ni stong nyid 'gyur/ /yang na thig le'i rnam pa la/ /spro ba dang ni bsdu ba dang/ /lnga ru lta dang
14a3(rgyud 'grel): gcig tu lta/ /rim gyis brtan par gyur nas ni/ /phyag rgya'i dngos grub thob pa'o/ /rdzogs pa'i rim pa'i sbyor ka ste bco brgyad pa'o// //
14a4(rgyud 'grel): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bgegs bskrad pa'i cho ga bstan pa/ /bgegs bskrad pa'i thabs la/ /cho ga che chung gi rim pa/ /bsgrub bya'i skabs dang sbyar te/ /thabs dpag tu med par bya'o//
14a5(rgyud 'grel): de la rdzas kyis bskrad pa dang/ /sngags kyi bskrad pa dang/ stang stabs kyis bskrad pa dang/ phyag rgyas bskrad pa dang/ ting nge 'dzin gyis bskrad pa dang/ yang na rdzas dang sngags kyis bskrad pa dang/
14a6(rgyud 'grel): rdzas dang stang stabs kyis bskrad pa dang/ rdzas dang phyag rgyas bskrad pa dang/ rdzas dang ting nge 'dzin gyis bskrad pa dang/ yang na sngags dang gnyis 'dus pa dang/ stang stabs dang
14a7(rgyud 'grel): gnyis 'dus dang/ phyag rgya dang gnyis 'dus dang/ ting nge 'dzin dang gnyis 'dus dang/ phyag rgya stang stabs gnyis 'dus dang/ bzhi ka la ni sbyar bar bya/ /phyag rgya la
14b1(rgyud 'grel): yang de bzhin te/ /ting nge 'dzin kyang de ltar bya/ /gnyis 'dus gsum 'dus bzhi 'dus su/ /thams cad kun la sbyar bar bya/ /yang na lnga 'dus kho nas bya/ /bgegs kyi rim pa 'ang lngar shes bya/ /
14b2(rgyud 'grel): sne gdon phra mo kun la ni/ /sbyor ba gcig pu kho nas bzlog /rgyal 'gong la sogs gdon la ni/ /sbyor ba gnyis kyis bzlog par bya/ /de bas mtho ba'i bgegs gnyis la/ /gsum dang bzhi ni bya
14b3(rgyud 'grel): ba yin/ /bgegs ni chen po thams cad la/ /sbyor ba lnga po kho nas bya/ /rdzas kyi bya thabs bstan pa ni/ /gu gul yungs kar sha chen dang/ /tshil chen dang ni thal chen dang/ /dur khrod sol pa
14b4(rgyud 'grel): grog mkhar sa/ /de la sogs pa'i rdzas rnams la/ /gzugs brnyan bca' bar bya ba 'am/ /brdeg pa'i rdzas su bya ba dang/ /bdag pa'i rdzas su bya ba dang/ /bsrung ba'i rdzas su bya ba ni/ /
14b5(rgyud 'grel): gla rtsi dang ni rma bya yi/ /rgyal mtshan klu la shis par bstan/ /yang na dur khrod chen po'i rdzas/ /rgyan cha rnams kyis byin brlabs la/ /bskon pas bsrung bar 'gyur ba yin/ /sku ni byin gyis brlabs nas
14b6(rgyud 'grel): su/ /bsrung bar de ni 'gyur ba yin/ /sku dang glegs bam la sogs pa/ /byin gyis brlabs nas mdun bzhag pas/ /bsrung bar de ni 'gyur ba yin/ /rdo rje dril sogs phyag mtshan la/ /byin gyis brlabs nas lag gzhag na/ /bsrung ba de ni
14b7(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur ba yin/ /khyad par mgon po nag po yi/ /sku ni byin brlabs bzhag pas su/ /bsrung bar de ni 'gyur ba yin/ /skud sngon mdung pa bdun byas pas/ /mgul tu bcings pas bsrung bar 'gyur/ /yang na smyag shar lcug ma yis/ /byabs pas de ni tshar gcod do//
15a1(rgyud 'grel): de la sogs pa'i mthun rdzas rnams/ /thams cad kyis ni bya ba yin/ /'khor lo bcas nas lus la gdags/ /bsrung ba'i mchog ni yin par gsungs/ /sngags kyis bskrad pa bstan pa ni/ /oM na mo nI lAM ba ra d+ha
15a2(rgyud 'grel): ra badzra pA Ni che ge mo hUM hUM phaT/ ces bskrad pa'o/ /mA ra ya/ phaT gdags pa ni bsad pa'o/ /yang na 'khrul 'khor sbyor ba bzhin du bya'o/ /oM na mo nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni mahA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye hUM hUM phaT/ ces bya ba dang
15a3(rgyud 'grel): spel te bya'o/ /sgrub bya'i ming gi mdza' la sreg byed kyi yi ge dang ldan pa ni/ bgegs zhi bar byed pa'i sngags so/ /ming gi mdza' la bsrung ba'i sngags dang ldan pa ni/ bsrung ba'i sngags so/ /ming gi mdza' la dgug pa
15a4(rgyud 'grel): dang/ dbang du bya ba'i sngags kyang shes par bya'o/ /sngon du bsnyen pa rdzogs pas ni/ /sngags rings kho nas bya ba yin/ /khyad par du ni klu la shis/ /yang na drag po'i sngags 'di ni/ oM mahA tsaN+Da re Sha na hUM hUM phaT ces
15a5(rgyud 'grel): bya ba dang spel te bya'o/ /yang na rgyud bzhin btub pa dang/ /mi btub pa yi rim pa ni/ /slob dpon so so'i gzhung lugs so/ /ji ltar mos pas 'grub par 'gyur/ /drag po'i 'khrul 'khor gzhan rnams kyang/ /man ngag
15a6(rgyud 'grel): gzhan gyis sbyor shes bya'o/ /stang stabs sbyor bas tshar bcad ni/ /mnyam pa'i stang stabs la sogs pa bco brgyad kyis tshar bcad pa dang/ /pheg rdob skor bu la sogs pa/ /gyad 'gros rnams kyis tshar bcad pa dang /
15a7(rgyud 'grel): g.yas brkyang la sogs pas tshar bcad pa dang/ de gsum gang yang rung bas bya'o/ /stang stabs kyi sbyor ba las shes bya'o/ /phyag rgya la sogs pa'i sbyor ba yang lag stabs la sogs pa'i sbyor ba la sogs pa shes par
15b1(rgyud 'grel): bya'o /ting nge 'dzin gyi thabs ni/ dang por bdag nyid phyag na rdo rje gtum khro 'bar ba/ mche ba gtsigs pa/ spyan dgrad pa/ gos sngon po gsol pa/ sku che ba/ yan lag rags pa/ g.yas bskum pa/ g.yon brkyang bas bgegs kyi
15b2(rgyud 'grel): snying gar mnan pa/ phyag g.yas pa'i rdo rje gsor ba las/ /'od zer 'phros pas/ rdo rje phra mo'i mtshon cha grangs med par brgyud mar byung nas/ spyi gtsug tu rgyab pas/ rkang pa'i mthil du 'byin pa/ hUM sgra dang zhags pa'i sgra bsgrags
15b3(rgyud 'grel): pas thams cad dang ngas shing brgyal par byed pa/ sku las khro bo dpag tu med pa byung pas/ bsgrub bya'i ba spu bu gar zhugs nas khrag 'jib par byed pa/ thugs ka nas khro bo dpag tu med pa byung nas/ bsgrub bya'i snying kar gdab?
15b4(rgyud 'grel): ba/ sku la me dpung byung nas sreg par byed pa/ zhal nas sngags kyi sgra brjod pas 'byung po thams cad par byed de/ /de lta bu'i khro bo gcig bsgoms la/ ye shes bstim/ byin gyis brlab/ dbang bskur la nus pa'i mthu can du
15b5(rgyud 'grel): bya'o/ /bgegs chen po bskrag pa yang/ cho ga pha mos mi thub ste/ dang po kho nar sngon du bsnyen pa'i cho ga rdzogs par byas la/ bdag nyid lha'i rnal 'byor du bskyed la/ bdud rtsi lnga dang ldan pa'i gtor ma gcig byin gyis brlabs
15b6(rgyud 'grel): la/ bde bar gshegs pa la dbul/ mthu bskyed la gsol pa gdab/ yang gtor ma gcig la thun mong gi rdzas dang ldan pa'i steng du/ khrag sna snying sna sha sna gsum dang ldan pa'i rdzas la/ byin gyis brlabs la chos skyong
15b7(rgyud 'grel): ba'i srung ma la phul la/ bdag gi stong grogs mdzad par las bsgo'o/ /gtor ma cha gcig la drug cu pa ldan pa'i rdzas la byin gyis brlabs la/ 'byung po thams cad la byin la/ gnod pa ma byed par bsgo par bya/ yang na zhi
16a1(rgyud 'grel): ba'i sbyin sreg gis bgegs zhi bar bya ste/ de ltar yang nas yang du byas pas bgegs zhi bar 'gyur ro/ /de ltar byas kyang 'gror ma btub na/ drag po'i las bya ste/ dang po kho nar bdag gi thugs ka nas
16a2(rgyud 'grel): khro bo'i sprul pa bgyi bas/ 'byung po thams cad bkug pa dang/ yang na nad pa nyid la bsams te/ yi ge gsum las 'phros 'dus pa las/ ri rab tu gyur nas/ ri rab snying gar mnan par bsam/ de ni mnan pa'i
16a3(rgyud 'grel): sbyor ba'o/ /bgegs bsreg pa ni/ yi ge hUM gi 'phro 'dus/ lce nag po rdo rje spu gu can du gyur nas/ de'i nang na tshur 'od zer me 'dra ba byung nas gang la gnod pa'i sar gtad la bgegs thams cad bsreg par bya ste/
16a4(rgyud 'grel): yang na lce rdo rje sngon por bsgyur la/ 'od zer sngon po rlung 'dra bas thams cad gtor zhing bskrad par bsam mo/ /yang na srog gi 'od zer 'phros pas/ bgegs thams cad bcom nas slar 'dus pas snying ka'i lha la mchod
16a5(rgyud 'grel): par bsam mo/ /yang na mdun gyi lha mchod par bsam mo/ /bsreg gtor bcom pa'i sbyor pa'o/ /yang na bsang pa'i sbyor ba ni/ gong gi sku bskyed pa la sogs pa man ngag sbyor ba yod pa rnams/ rim pa bzhin tu shes par bya'o/ /khyad par sbyor ba bstan pa ni/ thugs
16a6(rgyud 'grel): kyi 'od zer 'phro ba dang/ /gsung gi yig 'bru spro ba dang/ /sku yi sprul pa spro ba dang/ /yang na thugs kyi phyag mtshan yin/ /lte 'og gnas su bstim pa dang/ /gnas dgu dag tu bstim pa dang/ /thams cad kun tu
16a7(rgyud 'grel): bstim pa dang/ /de ltar bstim la lus dgang ngo/ /thur du bda' dang gyen du bda'/ /srog 'gro steng 'og bda' ba dang/ /'byung sa gnyis nas gdon pa dang/ /'ded pa'i tshul gyis bda' ba dang/ /bton nas bzhu
16b1(rgyud 'grel): btul bya ba dang/ /de nas lha la mchod pa bya/ /de la sogs pa'i man ngag gis/ /sbyor ba gzhan yang shes par bya/ /de lta'i sbyor ba byed pa yang/ /phal dang phal gyi thun mong min/ /lus kyi rgyan cha la sogs ldan/ /ngag gi ma nyams yon 
16b2(rgyud 'grel): tan ldan/ /bar chad rdul tsam ma shor bar/ dper na dul chu brub pa bzhin/ /de gsum gsal bar brjod pa yin/ /snod min pa la gsang 'gyur yin/ /dper na srin po dur skad bzhin/ /tshig mi gsal bar don gsal ba/ /yid
16b3(rgyud 'grel): brten drag tu bzla bar bya/ /de lta'i bgegs bskrad sbyor ba yang/ /thams cad kun la bya ba min/ /bsgom sgrub par chad byung ba dang/ /slob dpon gzhan don mdzad pa la/ /'byung pos bar chod byas pa la/ /sbyor ba 'di ni bya bar
16b4(rgyud 'grel): gsungs/ /rdo rje spun la bya ba yin/ /gzhan yang sems can gzhan po ni/ /mi dge spang zhing dge bcu spyod/ /de la'ang bya bar gsungs pa yin/ /gnyi ga mi byed sems can la/ /sbyor ba chung du bya bar gsungs/ /mi dge bcu
16b5(rgyud 'grel): ni dang len cing/ /rdo rje slob dpon la smod cing/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa 'jig pa dang/ /rgyal khams yongs su gnod pa dang/ /dge 'dun 'du ba'i sgo 'phrog dang/ /theg chen gsang sngags smod pa dang/ /rnal 'byor spyi yi dgrar
16b6(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur la/ /sbyor ba 'di ni byar mi rung/ /gal te sems can de dag kyang/ /gnod zhing 'gyod pas mthol bshags nas/ /sangs rgyas theg pa'i sgor 'jug cing/ /yang dang yang du gsol 'debs na/ /sbyar ba 'di ni bya bar gsungs/
16b7(rgyud 'grel): sbyor ba 'di yi man ngag kyang/ /rang gi srog bzhin ma btsos na/ /snod dang mi ldan la spel nas/ /be sbrel g.yang kar khrid pa bzhin/ /gcig lhung bas na gnyis ka lhung/ /de bas nan tan cher gyis la/ /rin chen lta bu'i
17a1(rgyud 'grel): gang zag la/ /bcas ka dam bzhag byas te gtad/ /bgegs bskrad pa la sogs pa'i sbyor ka ste bcu dgu pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje bsnams pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dug sngags kyi ni gtso bo bu/
17a2(rgyud 'grel): sngon du bsnyan pa bya ba'i phyir/ /sngon du bsnyen pa'i man ngag rnams/ /cung zhig bsdus te bstan par bya/ /dang po skad cig lhar bsams te/ /snying kar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor bsam/ /de steng hUM gi 'phro 'du yis/ /mchod pa la sogs
17a3(rgyud 'grel): rtogs byas nas/ /stong pa nyid du bsgom par bya/ /stong pa nyid kyi ngang las ni/ /paM las pad+ma 'dab ma brgyad pa bsam/ /pad+ma'i lte bar zla ba'i dkyil 'khor bsam/ /de steng haM gi 'phru 'du yis/ /rdo rje gur du gyur nas phyir/ /cho ga gsum
17a4(rgyud 'grel): mam skad cig mas/ phyag na rdo rje'i sku bskyed la/ /don du rdo rje sems shes bya/ /rdo rje bsnams dang chos nyid kyi/ /don la sems dpa' ye shes la/ /las su ming dang tha dad tsam/ /de nyid sku mdog dkar la 'cher/ /phyag gnyis
17a5(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje dril bu bsnams/ /rgyan rnams thams cad rdzogs ldan zhing/ /rdo rje skyil krung tshul du bzhugs /ye shes spyan drangs snying kar bstim/ /sku gsung thugs ni byin brlabs dbang bskur bya/ /de ltar brtan bsgoms thugs ka ru/ /zla ba
17a6(rgyud 'grel): pad+ma lte ba la/ /man ngag bzhin du bsgom par bya/ /de ltar gsal nas bzlas rjod bya/ /thugs 'khor gsal dang lha mchod dang/ /sbyang dang bsdu ba'i tshul bzhin du/ /'bum gsum bsnyen pa bya ba dang/ /dus dang grangs dang mtshan ma yi/ /
17a7(rgyud 'grel): bsnyen pa la sogs char phyin nas/ /de nas 'khor rnams so so la/ /'bum phrag re re bsnyen pa bya/ /'khor rnams bsnyen pa'i man ngag ni/ /mdun du pad+ma'i gdan bskyed de/ /skad cig klu brgyad sprul nas ni/ /spyan drangs la sogs rdzogs byas la//
17b1(rgyud 'grel): 'od zer 'phros pas mchod mnyes la/ /don rnams gang yin grub par bsam/ /gong bzhin mtshan ma'i rtags byin nas/ /de nas bsgrub pa brtsam par bya'o/ /lha bskyed la sogs cho ga ni/ bsnyen pa'i dus dang mthun par bya/ /gtso bo'i bzlas brjod 'bum phrag gcig /
17b2(rgyud 'grel): 'khor rnams khri dang stong dang ni/ /brgya yi bar du rab 'bring ngo/ /dug gis zin pa'i bsgrub bya ste/ /mdun sogs bya ba rdzogs byas la/ /lus kyi yan lag brgyad po la/ /yi ge dgong sogs bya ba ni/ /mgo rak+ShaM? sna dang rna bar yum/ /mig tu hUM dang khar ni suM/ /
17b3(rgyud 'grel): mgrin par smryuM snying gar ym? / /lte bar k? du shes par bya'o/ /kha dog dkar po bsam par bya/ /sngags rnams de yi mthus su ni/ /snying ga'i dug ni bcing bar bya/ /ye shes yi ge hUM gis ni/ /dug 'phros la sogs man ngag sbyar/ /de 'og phyi ma'i las brtsam mo/
17b4(rgyud 'grel): rin chen la sogs bum pa la/ /skyon bral yon tan ldan pa ru/ /chu dang 'o ma bsreg pas dgang/ /dang po bum ? bum bskyed la/ /pad+ma zla ba'i gdan stengs su/ /de steng yi ge su las ni/ /gyur pa'i rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/ /gdugs dkar gyis ni brgyan mdzad cing/
17b5(rgyud 'grel): sku mdog dkar po phyag gnyis pa/ kha TwAM thod pa phyag na bsnams/ /sbrul gyi rgyan dang ldan pa la/ /sems dpa' yi ni skyil krung bcas/ /klu rnams mgo bo'i cha rnams ni/ /zla ba'i dkyil 'khor 'og bsdus nas/ /de steng rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma/ /pad+ma yi ni 'dab ma
17b6(rgyud 'grel): la/ /klu chen brgyad po bsgom par bya/ /shar du nor rgyas bu dkar po/ byang du 'jog po ser po'o/ /nub tu stobs rgyu dmar po ste/ /lhor ni pad+ma sngon po'o/ /dbang ldan du ni pad+ma che/ /dkar ser du ni bsgom par bya/ /me mtshams su ni dung skyong dkar sngo'o/ /bden bral du ni
17b7(rgyud 'grel): rigs ldan sngo dmar po/ /rlung mtshams 'khyil pa dmar ser po/ /de ltar klu brgyad bsam pa ni/ /mchod dang gtor ma la sogs bya/ /de dus rdo rje mkha' 'gro ru/ /dug sel pa yi dus 'di ru/ /bdag nyid lha yi rnal 'byor bya/ /cho ga bskyed tshul thabs dang mthun
18a1(rgyud 'grel): rma bya'i sngo yi chun po yi/ /mgo bo la sogs lus kun la/ /byab cing man ngag sbyor shes bya'o/ /rkang mthil bar du drangs nas ni/ /bum pa'i nang du dpo bar bya/ /lha gsal la sogs man ngag bya/ /oM h+ri ta na da ra hUM phaT swAhA/ zhes bya ba man ngag tu/ hUM gsuM
18a2(rgyud 'grel): phaT gsum shes par bya/ /oM bA su ki h+ri ta na da ra swAhA/ oM hak+Sha ka h+ri ta na da ra swAhA/ phaT phaT phaT swAhA/ oM kor ko Ta h+ri ta na da ra swAhA/ oM pad+ma h+ri da na da ra swAhA/ oM mahA pad+ma h+ri da na da ra swAhA/ oM shaM ka bA la h+ri ta na da ra swAhA/ /oM ku li shA laM h+ri ta na da ra swAhA/ oM hu lu d+he ke li h+ri ta na da ra
18a3(rgyud 'grel): swAhA/ oM h+ri ta na da ra hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT/ a mu ka sa ni ra ba shaM ku ru hUM phaT swAhA/ oM ba su ki d+hi ha da ta na d+ha re de ba da ta ta ni ra ba shiM ku ru hUM hUM hUM phaT phaT phaT swAhA/ /bsnyen bsgrub la sogs bya ba yang/ /sngags kyi dbye ba la sogs kyang/ /man ngag can gyi ? shes bya/ /dug phrogs 'o ma ngag po
18a4(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur/ /de 'og yungs kar la sogs kyis/ sngags bzlas pas su rdeg par bya/ /brdeg pa tsam gyis bsgrub bya yi/ /snying ni 'bar ba la sogs 'gyur/ de yi snying gar yi ge hUM/ /bsdoms pas rnams shes bcings zhing gzung/ /de tsam gyis ni dbugs g.yo 'gyur/ /bdag gi sna
18a5(rgyud 'grel): sgo'i 'od zer gyis/ /mche bas zin pa'i sna sgor thim/ /lus bkang bas ni rkang lag 'dar/ /de nas hUM gi glu blang bya/ /de yang sngon du se gol tog/ gsum gyi snga yis ldang bar 'gyur/ /langs nas rdo rje mkha' 'gro bsgom/ /yan lag thams cad bsrung bar bya'o/ /klu sman dkar gsum sna tshogs kyis
18a6(rgyud 'grel): mchod dang gtor ma klu la shis/ /de sogs sbyor ba gzhan la yang/ /slob dpon mkhas pas sbyor shes bya/ /dug gis zin pa'i gnas brtan pa/ /kha dang smin ma rkan dang ni/ /sna rtse sna sgo mtshan ma dang/ /bshad pa mthe bong gzung ba rnams/ /gso ru mi rur spang bar bya/ /rigs ldan mgo brgya
18a7(rgyud 'grel): gcig pa dang/ /ka ma la ni dug gi mche ba ste/ /bzhis zin pa ni 'chi bar 'gyur/ /lhag ma rnams ni gsong rung bas/ /rnal 'byor snying rje dang ldan ba/ /dbang bskur man ngag ldan pa yis/ /cho ga gzhung bzhin byas pa dang/ /gzhan sgrol stobs kyis bdag kyang sgrol/ /dngos grub kyang ni thob bar
18b1(rgyud 'grel): gsungs/ /de bas brtson 'grus bskyed de bsgrub/ /mchod rten la sogs byas nas ni/ /lha gshegs ting 'dzin bsdu bar bya/ /de 'gro smon lam gdab bya ba/ /dper na sman rnams mthu yis ni/ /rdzas kyis dug ni ?? pa bzhin/ /de bzhin klu yi dug rnams ni/ /sngags kyi mthus
18b2(rgyud 'grel): su 'joms par 'gyur/ /rnam par rtog pa'i dug rnams ni/ /ye shes mthu yis 'joms par 'gyur/ /rdzas kyi mthu yis stobs rnams kyis/ /dug rnams ma lus zhi rgyur cig /sngags kyi mthu yi stobs rnams kyis/ /dug rnams ma lus zhi gyur cig /ye shes mthu yis stobs rnams kyis
18b3(rgyud 'grel): dug rnams ma lus zhi gyur cig /dug rnams zhi byed mthu yis ni/ /thams cad byang chub thob par shog /dug zhi bar byed pa'i ? ste nyi shu pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dgug pa la sogs sbyor ba bzhan yang bstan/ /lha bskyed sbyor
18b4(rgyud 'grel): ?? sngags rnams so so'i mdza' la ni/ dgug pa'i ? gdags par bya/ /yang na ga dA dzA dza dza zhes pas/ thun mong gi sngags su shes par bya'o/ /sngags kyi yi ge'i 'od zer gyis/ /gang 'dod gnas nas bkug nas ni/ /shing chen dag ni sdong po la/ /shing gi cho la ni byung nas su/ /? ga dag la klu
18b5(rgyud 'grel): gzugs bri/ /'od zer 'phros pas de la bkug/ de nas shing chen nang du gzhug /kha bcad tshon gyi skud pas bcing/ thal sogs 'dag pas zhal zhal bya/ /yang na pha bong la gong ma bzhin du shes par bya'o/ /de ltar mi bya ba skad pa ni/ /shing shun la sogs dag la ni/ /rlung dam sha ba'i
18b6(rgyud 'grel): gzugs bris la/ /de yi steng du bsgrub bya'i gzugs/ /gang 'dod pas ni bris nas bzhag rtsa sngags mdza' la bskrad sngags gdags/ /gang ltar 'dod pa'i sa phyogs su/ /sngags kyi 'od zer stobs kyis 'phang/ /gong gi sbyor bas bkug nas su/ /gru gsum nag po'i 'brub
18b7(rgyud 'grel): khung du/ /nag po'i sbyor bas kha bcad la/ /ri rab gzugs bri mnan pa bya'o/ /lha rnams bcu bdun stang stabs kyis/ /ji tsam 'dod par mnan par bya'o/ /bsad par 'dod pa'i sbyor ka yis/ /gzugs brnyan la sogs gong bzhin bca' / /bsnyen pa la sogs rdzogs pa yis
19a1(rgyud 'grel): gsang sngags la sogs shes byas la/ /mtshon cha phyag mtshan byin brlabs la/ /khro bo mtshon cha thogs pa yis/ /lus rnams gtud shing gsed par bsam/ /yang na 'khrul 'khor sbyor ba bya/ /yang na sngags kyi 'od zer gyis/ /gang 'dod par ni
19a2(rgyud 'grel): bsreg par bya/ /yang na sbyin sreg dag gis bya/ /dam la ma thogs klu rnams ni/ /sgrub pa po la bar chad byed/ /dang po zhi bas gdul bar bya/ /zhi bas 'dul bar ma gyur na/ /de la drag po'i las rnams brtsam/ /dam la thogs pa'i klu rgyal ni/ /de sten cing bsgrubs
19a3(rgyud 'grel): na dngos grub ster/ /bde gshegs sprul pa bsgrubs na ni/ /dngos grub mchog kyang ster par byed/ /klu rgyal der sgrub sbyor ba yang/ /sngon 'gro 'gro cho ga rdzogs nas ni/ /de nas stong ba nyid du bsgom/ /stong pa'i ngang las pad+ma'i gdan /de steng cho ga gsum
19a4(rgyud 'grel): kyis bskyed/ /lhag pa'i lha ni gang 'dod bskyed/ /gzhan dag sprul pa'ang gang 'dod pa yang yod/ /mdun ru bang zla'i gdan steng du/ /cho ga gsum 'am skad cig sprul/ /sku mdog dkar po sprul zhags bsnams/ /klu rgyal de 'dra spyan drangs bstim//
19a5(rgyud 'grel): mchod bstod la sogs rdzogs byas la/ /de nas gang yin bzlas brjod bya/ /klu'i sbyor ba ste nyi shu gcig pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnal 'byor bsnyen pa rdzogs pa yis/ /'khrul 'khor rim pa brtsam
19a6(rgyud 'grel): par bya/ /dang po las gzhi'i rim pa ni/ /zhi ba go ro tsa na blang/ /gro ga 'am stug ma'i shun pa la/ /rtsa sogs dkar po ma yin spangs/ /zhi bar 'dod pa snyu gu yis/ /bsgrub bya sgrub byed 'khor lo bri/ /'khor lo'i dkyil 'khor bri ba ni/ /brgyad dang bcu
19a7(rgyud 'grel): gnyis bcu drug bri/ /shes rab cho gas yang dag bri/ /yang na gcig dang gnyis su bya/ sngags ni thams cad dgod pa dang/ /gcig dang gnyis su dgod pa'o/ /yi ge re re dgod pa dang/ /thams cad rdzogs par dgod pa'o/ /shar nas brtsams te
19b1(rgyud 'grel): bri bar bya/ /de ma thag tu dor ba yang/ /bsgrub bya'i ming dang na ma dang/ /bskul pa'i tshig dang bcas par bri/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa'i sbyor ba yis/ /yi ge hUM gi 'od zer las/ /sngon po dkyil 'khor spyan drangs nas/ /mchod bstod bsnyen pa byas nas su/ /dkyil 'khor 'di la
19b2(rgyud 'grel): gzhug par bya/ /byin dang ldan pa'i lha nyid ni/ /yi ge'i gzugs las 'phros pas na/ /dkar po dan byed brtul zhugs can/ /mar dang sbrang rtsi dbus dkar nas/ /skud pa dkar po bcing bar bya/ /me tog dkar pos thun gsum du/ /zhi ba'i sems kyis gtong bar
19b3(rgyud 'grel): bya/ /bdag nyid sngon po'i dkyil 'khor ni/ bskyed pa'i rim pa gang dod bya/ /zhi ba'i dkyil 'khor dkar po la/ de yi mdun du bsgrub byin/ /pad+ma zla bar gnas pa ste/ /kha dog dkar po zla ba'i mdangs/ /bsgrub bya gnas par mthong nas ni/ /bum pa dkar po'i zla ba'i
19b4(rgyud 'grel): mdangs/ /bdud rtsi lngas ni bkang pa yis/ /dbang bskur pa ni bsam par bya/ /rdzogs sangs rgyas pa grangs med dbang/ thob nas bsgrub bya gang yin la/ /bdud rtsi spyi bor blug par bya/ /bdag nyid sngon po'i sbyor ba yis/ /sngags kyi 'od zer spros pa las/ /bsgrub bya
19b5(rgyud 'grel): mi mthun zhi par bya/ /de nas bzlas pa brtsam par bya/ /oM na mo nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni hUM phaT swAhA/ /che ge mo zhe bar gyis shig /na ma swAhA/ dug ni zhi bar 'dod pa ni/ /gur kum dag gis 'khor lo bri/ /dkar po'i phyogs kyi tshes gcig nas/ /nag po'i
19b6(rgyud 'grel): gcig tu las rnams 'grub/ /de ltar rnal 'byor sgrub pa pos/ /'khor lo'i man ngag yod pa na/ /the tshom med par bya nas ni/ /sngags ni nan tan cher bskyed na/ /nges pa kho nar 'grub par 'gyur/ /zhe ba'i 'khrul 'khor gyi sbyor ka ste nyi shu gnyis
19b7(rgyud 'grel): ba'o/ /bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas gzhan yang rgyas pa yi/ /thams cad sngon bzhin byas nas ni/ /sngags ni thams cad dgod pa na/ /mi dgod pa ni sngon bzhin bya/ /'khor lo yang ni sngon bzhin no/ /stong pa'i mtshams
20a1(rgyud 'grel): ni blangs nas su/ /ming dang bskul tshig swAhA spel/ /gzhi ni gro ga? ma ras la bya/ /gur kum kha tshe skyes la sogs/ /gang 'dod pa yis bri bar bya/ /kham phong ser po kha sbyar nas/ /skud pa ser po bcing bar bya/ /bdag nyid rgyas pa'i lha nyid du/ /bskyed
20a2(rgyud 'grel): pa la sogs rdzogs par bya/ /yi ge hUM ni ser po yis/ /lcags kyu'i dbyibs 'dra spros nas ni/ /rgyas pa'i dkyil 'khor bkug nas ni/ /sngon zhing mchod pa la sogs bya/ /de nas 'khrul 'khor dag la bstim/ /byin dang ldan pa'i lha rnams ni/ /yi ge gzugs las
20a3(rgyud 'grel): 'od 'phros bas/ /ser po'i byed pa brtul zhugs can/ /mar dang sbrang rtsis snod bkang la/ /skud pa ser pos bcing bar bya/ /me tog ser pos thung sum du/ /rgyas pa'i sems kyis gtor zhing mchod/ /bdag nyid sngon po'i dkyil 'khor ni/ /cho ga gang 'dod la sogs bya/ /yi
20a4(rgyud 'grel): ge gzugs su mthong byas la/ /bsgrub pa'i mi mthun rgyas byas te/ /me tog ser po dus su mchod/ /lha yi rnal 'byor shes pa yis/ /thams cad rdzogs nas dkyil 'khor la/ /pad+ma zla ba'i gdan stengs su/ /bsgrub bya ser po bdun bsams la/ /gser sogs bum pas ?
20a5(rgyud 'grel): bskur bya/ /rgyas pa'i mi mthun skyon rnams ni/ /bkru zhing de nyid rgyas par bsam/ /sngon du gsungs pa'i sa bon las/ /me tog ser pos dus gsum du/ /sngags bzlas skyon rnams sbyang bar bsam/ /oM na mo nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni hUM/ che ge mo mo oM che ge mo oM che ge mo rgyas
20a6(rgyud 'grel): bar gyis shig swAhA/ /rgyas pa'i dus ni yang dag bstan/ /nya dang de bzhin rgyas pa'i nya/ /de yi dus su yang dag sbyar/ /rgyas pa'i las ni 'di dag la/ /rnal 'byor can gyis brtson par bya'o/ /rgyas pa'i 'khrul 'khor gyi sbyor ka ste nyi shu rtsa gsum pa'o// //
20a7(rgyud 'grel): bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas dbang gi 'khrul 'khor ni/ /gra ba dmar po'i rdzas rnams la/ /'khor lo gnyis ni sngon bzhin bri/ /sngags sogs dgod pa sngon bzhin bya/ /bsnyen pa yang ni sngon bzhin bya/ /rgya skyegs tsandan khu ba'am/ /srin lag
20b1(rgyud 'grel): khrag gis bri bar bya/ /kham phor nag po la ? min/ /kha sbyar 'khor lo gzhug par bya/ /sbrang rtsi mar gyis bkang nas su/ /skud pa dmar gyis bcing bar bya/ /lha yi rnal 'byor ldan pa yis/ /'od 'phros spyan drangs sngon bzhin mchod/ /de nas 'khor lo dag la bstim//
20b2(rgyud 'grel): dbang du byed pa'i lha rnams ni/ /sngags kyi gnas su nus mthu can/ /'od zer dmar po'i sbyor ba yis/ /bsgrub bya dbang du bya bar bsam/ /me tog dmar pos dus gsum mchod/ /cho ga las bskyed rdo rje 'dzin/ /dmar po kha dog dbang du byed/ /nub phyogs ngos
20b3(rgyud 'grel): su kha bltas la/ /zla ba dmar po dag la ni/ /bsgrub bya bsam bar byas nas ni/ /snying ga'i yi ge 'od zer gyis/ /bsgrub bya gnas pas bkug bsams la/ /khri yi sngags ni bzlas par bya/ /bsgrub bya'i lus la phog 'gyur bas/ /de yi sems ni yengs gyur nas/
20b4(rgyud 'grel): zhabs kyi drung du 'gyel bar bsam/ /skra grol ba la gos med pa/ /shin tu g.yeng ba'i bsgrub bya bsam/ /dbang du mi 'gyur gang yang med/ /oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni mahA tsaN+Da ro Sha na hUM hUM phaT/ che ge mo dbang du bgyis pas sa ma ya ho/ /gang dag dbang du mi
20b5(rgyud 'grel): 'gyur pa/ /kha ti ma yi me naM du ba med/ /sngags bzlas 'khrul 'khor la ni bsro/ /las su bya ba dus bstan pa/ /nag po'i brgyad nas brtsams nas ni/ /de bzhin nag po'i brgyad kyi bar/ /brtul zhugs can gyis dbang la sbyor/ /de bzhin dbang gi 'khrul 'khor la//
20b6(rgyud 'grel): rnam 'byor can gyis brtson par bya'o/ /dbang gi 'khrul 'khor gyi sbyor ka ste nyi shu bzhi pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje bsnams pa phyag 'tshal lo/ /drag po yi ni 'khrul 'khor dag /dur khrod dag gi ras ma la/ /ske tshe nim pa'i bye brag gis/ /tsha
20b7(rgyud 'grel): pa gsum gyi mar dang dur khrod sol/ /d+ha d+hu ra dang gtum po'i sa bon dang/ /khro mdzub khrag dang tsi ta khu ba dang/ /byi brun gyis ni 'jim pas blang/ /gtum byed kyi ni phru ba'i chus/ /ltogs chen sgro yi smyu gu yis/ /bdag nyid lha yi rnal 'byor ldan/ /gtuM
21a1(rgyud 'grel): po khros pa'i sa bon gyis/ /brtul zhugs can gyis 'khor lo gis/ /bcu yi nyi ma phyed na bri/ /sngags la sogs pa dgod pa ni/ /sngon du gsungs pa'i rnam pa ni/ /de nas stong pa'i ling tshe rnams/ /ming dang bskul tshig hUM phaT ldan/ /rnal
21a2(rgyud 'grel): 'byor khros pa'i gzugs can gyis/ /'od zer 'phros pas lha rnams dgug /cho ga la sogs byas pha la/ /de nas bkug ste 'khor lor gzhug /gsod dang ldan pa'i khro bo ni/ /nus dang ldan pa'i yi ge rnams/ /gdug pa'i tshogs kyis bsad par bya/ /de ltar byin gyis
21a3(rgyud 'grel): brlab par bya/ /byi brun 'jim pa gtum byed chus/ /kham por sbyar zhing dgang bar bya/ /me tog nag pos dus gsum mchod/ /bdag nyid khros pa'i rnal 'byor gyis/ /lho phyogs kha bltas bsgrub bya mdun/ /'brub khung la sogs man ngag rdzogs/ /gzugs
21a4(rgyud 'grel): brnyan mdun du bzhag nas ni/ /bsad pa'i man ngag la sogs bya/ /gnas der bdag nyid sbyor ldan pas/ /rgyal rigs thod pa'am gzhan yang rung/ /nang gi 'bru dang sman ngag dang/ /glang rta mi khrag thod pa bkang/ /bkang ste thod pa gsum bskyed bzhag /
21a5(rgyud 'grel): dur khrod dag gis ro shing bskul/ /khros pa'i me yis bskul bar bya/ /dur khrod ras mar bsgrub bya'i ming gzugs bri/ /steng gi thod par bcug ste bzhag /thod pa kha sbub thal ba phyogs su gtor/ /'dis ni nges par gsod par 'gyur/ /yang na gzhan sogs sbyor
21a6(rgyud 'grel): ba ni/ mkhas pa yis ni shes par bya/ /oM nI lAM bar d+ha ra badzra pA Ni mahA yak+Sha se nA pa ta ye hUM hUM phaT phaT/ de ba da ta ta mA ra ya hUM phaT/ drag po'i 'khrul 'khor gyi sbyor ka ste nyi shu lnga pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin pa la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de nas
21a7(rgyud 'grel): bskrad pa'i 'khrul 'khor brtsam/ /dur khrod ras ma khru gang la/ /mngon du gsungs pa'i rdzas rnams kyis/ /'khor lo'i sngags sogs sngon bzhin bri/ /stong pa'i ling tshe blangs nas ni/ /gang ming bskul ba'i sngags dang ldan/ /bdag nyid lha yi sbyor sogs ldan
21b1(rgyud 'grel): 'od zer 'phros nas spyan drangs mchod/ /gsol bstod byas nas bsnyen pa bya/ /khri ni thos nag po'i phyogs/ /nag po'i phyogs kyi tshes bzhi la/ /gsol ba btab ste bstod pa bya/ /them pa'am rgya gram lam du spa/ /bsgrub bya ji srid mnan pa ru/ /'thab cing 'thab pas dbye
21b2(rgyud 'grel): bar bsam/ /gtor ma byin nas skrod cig ces/ /gsol ba mang du gdab par bya/ /khros pas nub byang kha bltas te/ /sngags bzlas myur bar 'bros par 'gyur/ /khyim du rtag tu 'thab 'bros pa/ /oM nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra badzra pA Ni mahA yak+Sha sa nA pa ta ye hUM hUM phaT phaT/ de ba da ta ta che ge mo skrod

25b5(rgyud 'grel): nas ni/ /lha yi nga rgyal ldan pa yis/ /dang po bum pa byin gyis brlab/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sngags kyis gdab/ /oM a mri ta kun Da li hUM/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig bdun du gdab/ /gong gi bkra shis snod kyi rdzas/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil bas btab nas kyang/ dang po bum pa'i chus su
25b6(rgyud 'grel): bsang?/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sngags kyang bzlas/ /thugs ka'i a las zla ba yi/ /dkyil 'khor chen po nyid du bsam/ /oM a tsan+d+ra maN+Da la hUM/ /bdun dang lnga dang gsum du bzlas/ /tsandan las gyi bum pa bsam/ /yi ge du 'phros tsandan phog /de las ma 'phros pas maN+Dal/
25b7(rgyud 'grel): ?? /oM d+hu ba spha ra Na hUM/ zhes pa lan bdun bzlas so/ /me tog lnga dang gnyis gcig la/ /kha dog mtshan nyid shes byas la/ /yi ge paM las pad+ma ni/ /stong ldan brgyad ldan dag tu ni/ /gyur par bsams nas sngags bzlas dgram/ /oM paM pad+ma maN+Dal hUM/ zhes gong ma bzhin
26a1(rgyud 'grel): du brjod par bya'o/ /de steng b+h+ruM las gzhal yas khang/ /lnga dang gnyis dang gcig tu bya/ /de nas thams cad kun la yang/ /gsum du bya bar 'dod pa'ang yod/ /zla ba pad+ma gzhal yas khang/ /gsum dang gnyis dang gcig tu yang/ /rnal 'byor bsdus dang
26a2(rgyud 'grel): rgyas pa ni/ nyams pa che chung go rims so/ /de nas rnal 'byor bdag nyid dang/ /dam tshig nyams pa'i rnal 'byor kun/ /khrus byas gos ni bzang po gon/ /rgyan cha la sogs mdzes par bya/ /shar ram nub tu kha bltas te/ /so so lha yi ting 'dzin bskyed/ /rdo rje dril bu byin
26a3(rgyud 'grel): gyis brlab/ /rdo rje dril bus bskul nas byang/ /tshigs bcad dag gis gsol ba btab/ /sngags kyi rgyal po mdza' la gdags/ /thugs ka'i zla ba'i dkyil 'khor du/ /yi ge bzhi 'phros lha mor gyur/ /bla ma yi dam lha dang ni/ /gsang sngags bdag po dkyil 'khor lha
26a4(rgyud 'grel): dkon mchog gsum sogs spyan drangs nas/ /bla ma sbyangs nas mi bskyod 'gyur/ /mchod yon mchod sogs rgyas par dbul/ /de yi sngon du phyag rnams bya/ /gzhan yang mchod pa sna tshogs kyis/ /mchod nas bstod pa rgyas par bya'o/ /de nas sngags bzlas 'od
26a5(rgyud 'grel): zer gyis/ /lha rnams la ni phog nas su/ /'od zer bskul nas tshur la 'dus/ /nyams pa'i lus la phog nas su/ /ba spu'i khung zhugs sdig pa bsdus/ /snying khar yi ge kaM ngam ni/ /'od nag tu ni gyur par bsam/ /srog go 'dus kyi sna nas byung/ /lha dang
26a6(rgyud 'grel): bdag gi bar du ni/ /pad+ma nag po'i gdan bsams la/ /sdig pa'i gzugs de de ru bzhag /de nas yi dam lha yi sngags/ /bzlas pa'i 'od zer 'khrul 'khor gyis/ /sdig pa rnams ni sbyang bar bya/ /yang na/ sdig pa de nyid sbyangs na kyang/ lus kyi lhag ma sbyang ba 'am/ /de
26a7(rgyud 'grel): nas yi ge brgya pa yis/ /man ngag bzhin du bsgoms nas kyang/ /snga ma bzhin du sbyang bar bya/ /yang na/ yi ge brgya pa gcig pus bya/ /yi ge brgya pa 'bum dang ni/ /rang gi snying po 'bum gyis ni/ /rtsa ba nyams pa chen po skongs/ /sum cha phri bas gnyis pa skongs/ /phyed? gyi
26b1(rgyud 'grel): bas ni gsum pa bskangs/ /sum gnyis phri bas bzhi pa skangs/ /sum cha'i sum cha phri bas ni/ /lnga pa skongs te drug pa ni/ /sum gnyis phri bas skongs pa'o/ /de yi phyed phyed phri bas ni/ /tha ma gsum gyis go rim sbyor/ /yan lag brgyad dang brgya phyed dang/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig
26b2(rgyud 'grel): dag gis so/ /che chung rim pa dag gis ni/ /tha ma me 'am chu yis ni/ /sbyin sreg dag gis sbyin par bya/ /gsang sngags bdag gam bdud rtsi 'khyil/ /rta mgrin bum pa gong bzhin bcas/ /byin rlabs la sogs byas nas ni/ /tha ma dag par bkru ba'o/ /sbyin sreg khrus
26b3(rgyud 'grel): dang ldan pa 'am/ /yang na maN+Dal bzlas pa yis/ /tshig gcig pus byed yang bya/ /dam tshig nyams pa bskang pa yi/ /sbyor ka 'di la brtson par bya'o/ /dam tshig nyams pa bskang pa'i sbyor ka ste nyi shu dgu pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag
26b4(rgyud 'grel): 'tshal lo/ /dbang gi rim pa bstan pa ni/ /bum pa gsang ba ye shes dang/ /bzhi par bstan pa de rnams la/ /gnas ni yid 'ong la sogs su/ /dus la sogs pa mjom pa dang/ /slob dpon slob ma mtshan nyid ldan/ /sngon gyi gleng gzhi rjes mthun par/ /dkyil 'khor
26b5(rgyud 'grel): byas nas slob ma gzhug /dbang bskur rim pa mnod bar/ /rnam grangs rnams ni shes par bya/ /bskur thabs man ngag shes byas la/ /bskur ba'i gnas kyang mnor brtag /de ltar byas pas sgrib par byang/ /sa yang rim gyis non par 'gyur/ /de phyir man ngag
26b6(rgyud 'grel): bstan par bya/ /rtags la sogs pa'ang shes par bya/ /brda' mi shes na sngags pa min/ /las dang po yis rdzas la brten/ /dgos pa shes na the tshom med/ /nus pa mthu dang ldan pas ni/ /'bras bu khyad par thob par 'gyur/ /de dag spyi dang khyad par ni/ /cho ga man ngag
26b7(rgyud 'grel): rgyas pa rnams/ /rgyud 'grel kun na gsal bas na/ /'di ru bdag gis mdo tsam bsdus/ /bum pa'i dbang ni rnam bzhi ste/ /phyi dang nang dang gsang ba dang/ /mthar thug pa ru shes par bya/ /phyi ni phyi rgyud dag dang mthun/ /nang ni nang rgyud dag dang mthun/ /yang na gnyis ka phyi
27a1(rgyud 'grel): ru bstan/ /nang gi slob dpon lus la bzhag /gsang ba yul ni nyid la sbyar/ /mthar thug slob ma mgo bo ru/ /dga' ba bskyed ba'am rdo rje'i rtsa/ /de rnams man ngag rgyas bshad ba/ /las kyi phreng bar shes par bya/ /gsang ba dbang la bzhi ru bstan//
27a2(rgyud 'grel): phyi ni bdud rtsi byin rlabs sbyin/ /yang na mtshan ldan phab nas ni/ /srin mtheb dag gis sbyin par bya/ /nang gi gsang ba pho brang nas/ /lag pa'i phyag rgya gzung nas sbyin/ /gsang ba yum gyi mkha' nas blang/ /mthar thug gsang ba'i pho brang du/ /mchog dga' skyes
27a3(rgyud 'grel): par shes par bya/ /shes rab ye shes la yang bzhi/ /phyi ni las ni phyag rgya ma/ /nang ni 'od kyi rig ma yin/ /gsang ba bya gdong mal bya/ mthar thug dregs 'dzin gtum mo yin/ /mthar thug la ni gnyis su bstan/ /rtan bcas dang ni rten med do/ /rten med la yang gnyis
27a4(rgyud 'grel): su bstan/ /spros bcas dang ni spros med do/ /dbang gi man ngag rgyas bshad ba/ /slob dpon zhal gyi man ngag dang/ /las kyi phreng bar shes bar bya/ /brda' yi cho ga mdo tsam bstan/ /ka la sha a b+hi She ka zhes pa ni/ /bum pa'i dag brda' lus kyi brda'/ /lag ba'i sor mo
27a5(rgyud 'grel): bskongs nas ni/ /rtse mo bsdus pa'i bum pa'i tshul/ /gu hya a b+hi She ka zhes pa/ /gsang pa'i ngag brda lus kyi brda'/ /sdom pos khro mo gnon pa ni/ /lag pa 'drin shes par bya/ /pra dz+nyA dz+nyA na gu hya a b+hi She ka zhes pa ni/ /shes rab ye shes ngag gi brda'/ /lus
27a6(rgyud 'grel): kyi brda' ni lha sbyin brda'/ /yang na khyad par dga' ba mtshon/ /pra dz+nyA dz+nyA na gu hya a b+hi She ka zhes pa ni/ /bzhi pa'i ngag brda lus kyi brda'/ /lhan cig dga' ba skyes sa ru/ /mthe bo bcug nas mtshon par bya'o/ /de ltar brda rnams ma shes na/ /mkha' 'gro dngos
27a7(rgyud 'grel): grub ster ba na/ /brda rnams dris nas ster bar byed/ /brda rnams mi shes slar la 'tshor/ /yang na brda rnams gzhan po yang/ /me shes na ni mkha' 'gros gsong/ /brda la sogs pa ma shes na/ /gsang sngags sbyod pa'i dus dang ni/ /'byung po nyams sod gsal ba dang//
27b1(rgyud 'grel): mu? stegs shan 'dres 'byung ba dang/ /phyag dang phyag gi lan dus su/ /brda mi shes na sngags pa min/ /dbang bskur ba yi rim pa yang/ /chags lam grol lam gnyis shes bya'o/ /dbang bskur med na 'bras bu med/ /de bas dbang bskur nan tan bya/ /dbang gi sbyor ka ste
27b2(rgyud 'grel): sum cu pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dam tshig rnams ni cung zhig bstan/ /dang po spyod pa'i dam tshig ni/ /chags lam spyod lam grol lam spyod/ /de ltar gnyis ka spyod pa la/ /dang po mchog dang rab mchog go /de la yang ni phyi
27b3(rgyud 'grel): nang ngo/ /dang po phyi yi spyod dus su/ /yul dang dus kyi gnas skabs kyis/ /zhi bas 'dul dang drag pos 'dul/ /mthun 'jug spyod pa mkhas shing zab/ /zas dang gos sogs thams cad kyang/ /rang dang gzhan ni gnyis ka la/ /phan sems spyod pas 'jug bya'o//

27b5(rgyud 'grel): lam pas byin gyis brlabs/ /de ltar byin brlabs bdud rtsi blta/ /thams cad lha bsgoms mchod byas na/ /bsod nams chen po thob bar 'gyur/ /khyi phag spyod pa bzhin byas na/ /dam tshig nyams te yi dags sa/ /chang ni bdud rtsi chen po ste/ /btung bar
27b6(rgyud 'grel): bya ba kho na yin/ /zhes rgyud las gsungs pa ste/ /mtshan dang ldan pa'i snod mchog tu/ /rul sogs skyon rnams spangs pa yi/ /bdud rtsi ro ldan snod bkang ste/ /bdag nyid lha yi rnal 'byor bya/ /a las ka pA la ni bskyed/ /zla ba dang ni de yis bskyed/ /ha sa
27b7(rgyud 'grel): ni gzugs sogs rnam rtog sbyangs/ /h+ri(rgyud 'grel): sa ni ro sogs rnam rtog sbyangs/ /ho(rgyud 'grel): sa ni bdud rtsi chen por bzhu/ /mthe bong hUM las gzhi'i tshul/ /srin mtheb sum las ri rab tshul/ /bar na maM 'phros bdud rtsi bkug /bdag gzhan lha ni mchod byas pas//
28a1(rgyud 'grel): bsod nams chen po thob par 'gyur/ /de ltar ma byas glang chen bzhin/ /chags shing brkams sogs myos 'thur na/ /skye ba lnga brgyar smyon par skye/ /byin gyis brlabs pa'i rim pa yang/ /yang rigs lnga yi sbyor sogs bya/ /yang na mA ma kI yis sbyang//
28a2(rgyud 'grel): yang na bdud rtsi 'khyil sogs bya/ /mtshan ldan snod du chos 'byung dang/ /zla ba la sogs bsam byas la/ /mchod par bya ba'am yang na bdun/ /spyi gtsug bla ma bzhag byas la/ /sku gsung thugs ni gnas gsum bzhag /de nas 'thor zhing mchod pa yis/ /phyag
28a3(rgyud 'grel): rgya sngags kyis dbul bar bya/ /so so'i rtsa ba'i sngags la a mri ta kuN Da li zhes pa'am/ /a mri ta khA hi zhes ba gang yang rung/ /gsum gsum kun la dbul bar bya/ /de nas rang snying lta gsal la/ /ci ran gnod pa med tsam btung/ /nad la gnod par
28a4(rgyud 'grel): gyur kyang ni/ /thigs pa gsum ni dam tshig go /grol bas kyang ni mchod pa yi/ /dus su btung bar bya phyir ni/ /yul dus gnas skabs sbyar te btung/ /btung ba la sogs gzhan po yang/ /bdud rtsi ma byas 'thur byed pa/ /yi dags gnas su skye bar 'gyur/ /
