28a6(rgyud 'grel): ye shes skye pa sogs 'byung phyir/ /dam tshig tu ni bstan pa yin/ /yang na bskyed rim bstan pa dang/ /rlung rnams las su rung 'gyur na/ /phyag rgya'i dngos grub myur 'dod phyir/ /phyag rgya la ni brten par bya/ /rnal 'byor grol ba'i lam pas ni/ /yid kyi lha mo
28a7(rgyud 'grel): gzugs mdzes ma/ /mchod pa'i dus su dam tshig go /de nas mkha' 'gro lung ston dus/ /dngos grub myur du thob 'dod na/ /mkha' 'gro'i man ngag la brten no/ /de ltar go rims ma shes na/ /dam tshig nyams te srin bur skye/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa 'jigs pa
28b1(rgyud 'grel): la/ 'khrul 'khor sbyor ba shes bzhin du/ /mi rtsom pa ni dam tshig nyams/ /mi shes gnod pa mi byed la/ /byed na yang ni dam tshig nyams/ /de sogs sbyor ba gzhan po yang/ /man ngag gis ni shes par bya/ /mchog gi spyod pa'i dus su ni/ /brtul zhugs smon pa lkugs
28b2(rgyud 'grel): pa dang/ /gcer bu la sogs dus skabs sbyar/ /de ltar ma shes dam tshig nyams/ /rab mchog gi ni dus dag tu/ /don dam rang bzhin med pa 'am/ /sgyu ma'i ting 'dzin la brten nas/ /rdzogs pa'i ting 'dzin dus su ni/ /spyod pa la sogs byed pa ni/ /dam tshig nyams
28b3(rgyud 'grel): te thogs? chung ngo/ /mthun 'jug spyod pa 'gal ba med/ /lta ba'i dam tshig bstan pa ni/ /chos rnams sems kyi 'khrul pa ste/ sems las ma gtogs chos rnams med/ /chos su snang ba 'khrul ba'i sems/ /sems nyid de yang skye med phyir/ /yod med
28b4(rgyud 'grel): mdza' las 'das pa'o/ /bsam du med cing brjod du med/ /dper na nam mkha' ji bzhin no/ /lta spyod kyi dam tshig gi sbyor ka steng? sum cu gcig pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rab gnas cho ga bstan pa bya/ /sku
28b5(rgyud 'grel): gzugs la sogs kun la ni/ /rab tu gnas pa ma byas na/ /mu stegs lha rten bcas dang 'dra'o/ /rigs dang na tshod med pa'i mi/ /thams cad kun gyis bkur mi byed/ /de bzhin 'dir yang sku sogs la/ phyag la sogs pa byas gyur kyang/ bsod nams chen po thob mi 'gyur
28b6(rgyud 'grel): bsod nams chen po thob 'dod na/ rab gnas byas pas thob par 'gyur/ /de bas rab gnas bya ba gces/ /slob dpon mtshan nyid ldan pa yi/ /sngon du bsnyen pa bya ba ni/ /so so rang rang bsnyen pa bya/ /de ltar mi 'grub rnal 'byor pas/ /shAka thub bsnyen pa kun gyi ma/
28b7(rgyud 'grel): rdo rje 'dzin pa'i bsnyen pa yis/ /gsang sngags thun mong bstan pa yi/ /bsnyen pa rnam gsum rdzogs byas la/ /de nas sa chog la sogs pa/ /gzhan dang mthun par rgyas par bya/ /maN+Dal byi dor legs byas la/ /rgyan dang rol mo la sogs dgram//
29a1(rgyud 'grel): lha yi sta gon rdzogs byas la/ /de nas bum pa'i sta gon bya/ /maN+Dal me tog bcal bkram la/ /bdag nyid lha ru bsgoms nas su/ /yungs kar nim pa lag gnyis kyis/ /blangs nas gsum gsum mer bstab bya/ /oM sarba pA paM de? ha na badzrA ya/
29a2(rgyud 'grel): sarba pA paM da ha na badzra swAhA/ /chu snyim pa bkang pa lan gsum blugs/ /bla mas zan chu bsre snod thogs/ /lan gsum byabs te mer bcas rnams/ /phyi rol dag tu bskyal bar bya/ /nam mkha' lha bkang spos thogs nas/ /dkyil 'khor lha la gsol ba gdab/ /rig sngags
29a3(rgyud 'grel): rgyal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes tshigs bcad la sogs bsgrags par bya'o/ /de nas maN+Dal steng du ni/ /sku gdung la sogs bzhag byas la/ /slob dpon nub tu gnas nas ni/ /oM hUM baM a zhes brjod pas/ /ba yi rnam lnga gang yin pa/ /de ni mar chu sbyar ba dang/ /dri
29a4(rgyud 'grel): zhim tsandan chu nyid dang/ /'dag chal shing shun chu gsum ni/ /byin brlabs dur bas rim bzhin bsku/ /u dum ba ra b+ha ra tra dang/ /tsa ba le ke na dang ni/ /a shwad byang chub shing gang rnyed/ /zhib btags chur sbyar snod g.yas bzhag/ de nas khrus rnams rim
29a5(rgyud 'grel): par bya/ /de la sogs pa'i cho ga yis/ /sku gzugs sta gon gnas par bya/ /de nas dkyil 'khor bsgrub par bya/ /de rjes rab gnas brtsam par bya/ /sku rnams so so'i sa bon las/ /cho ga gsum sogs gang 'dod bskyed/ /ye shes lha yang so sor bstim/ /sku 
29a6(rgyud 'grel): gdung bstan par bskyed cing bstim/ /glegs bam so so'i snying po 'am/ /yang na A li kA li 'am/ /so so'i dkyil 'khor dag kyang rung/ /lha khang la sogs kun la yang/ /so so'i dkyil 'khor gang 'dod bya/ /yang na/ yi ge b+h+ruM ni rten yin la/ /de la brten pa gang
29a7(rgyud 'grel): 'dod pa'o/ /rdo rje dril bu dag la ni/ /hUM dang a yis sa bon las/ /d+harma a badzra hUM zhes/ /sngags kyis bskyed pa byas nas ni/ /phyag mtshan lha ni gang 'dod bstim/ /phyag mtshan la sogs gzhan la yang/ /phyag mtshan snying po lha gsum dang/ /sgrub pa po yi
29b1(rgyud 'grel): las dang sbyar/ /phreng ba la yang de bzhin no/ /mtshan ldan yi ge a yin no/ /rgyan dang rgyan cha la sogs pa/ /byin gyis brlab pa tsam ni bya/ /de dag thams cad kun la yang/ /bskyed dang bstim pa byas nas ni/ /de nas byin brlabs dbang bskur bya/ /de nas mchod lnga dbul
29b2(rgyud 'grel): par bya/ /de 'og lA sya la sogs brgyad/ /mchod pa nyi shu po yang bya/ /gos dang rgyal mtshan la sogs pa/ /rin chen bkra shis sgra dang ni/ /rol mo la sogs cho ga rnams/ /rgyas par phul nas bstod pa bya/ /de nas bzlas brjod ci ran bya/ /spyan 'byed sngags la sogs
29b3(rgyud 'grel): pa ni/ /klog phreng rgyud du shes par bya/ /yang na phyag mtshan la sogs kyi/ /cho ga bsdus par shes par bya/ /shin tu bsdus pa'i cho ga sogs/ /byin gyi brlabs la sogs pa tsam/ /de ltar rab gnas zin nas ni/ /bla ma mkhas pa de la ni/ /ci bod g.yon rnams dbul
29b4(rgyud 'grel): bar bya/ /des ni bsod nams chen po thob/ /ji ltar phongs par gyur yang ni/ /mchod pa'i yo byad rnams ni dbul/ /ser sna can ni dbul mi nus/ /des ni sdig 'phel bsod nams med/ /rab gnas bzang po zin nas ni/ /rang gnas bzang por gshegs su gsol/
29b5(rgyud 'grel): rab tu gnas pa'i sbyor ka ste sum cu gnyis pa'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'dzin la phyag 'tshal lo/ /'chi ba blu ba'i man ngag ni/ /'chi rtags rnam par bstan pa dang/ /'chi blu cho ga rgyas pa rnams/ /'chi blu chen por shes par bya/ /'dir ni bsgrub pa
29b6(rgyud 'grel): don du ni/ /gos sngon 'chi ba blu ba mchog/ /man ngag cung zhig bkol nas bstan/ /spyir ni 'chi ba blu ba la/ /dge ba'i phyogs ni mdza' yas mchog /gang byas kyang ni zlogs par 'gyur/ /gos sngon 'chi blu'i rim pa yang/ /nad pa sems ni dag pa yis//
29b7(rgyud 'grel): gos sngon na rgyud man ngag can/ /mkhas pa de ni spyan drangs la/ /gnas khang dgon par maN+Dal bya/ /maN+Dal byas pa'i 'og tu ni/ /rgyan rnams ma lus dgram par bya/ /nad pa la ni chos bshad la/ /dang po sems ni dag par bya/ /sgyu ma lta bu'i sems
30a1(rgyud 'grel): kyis ni/ /nor rnams ma lus thams cad dang/ /rang lus srog dang bcas pa dbul/ /de ltar dbul ba de la ni/ /dang po dbang bskur rdzogs pa la/ /de nas man ngag gzhan sogs bya/ /de ltar byas 'og sos 'gyur la/ /rang 'tsho rdzas tsam slar la sbyin/ /nor
30a2(rgyud 'grel): rdzas srog rnams dbul mi nus/ /ser sna can ni bzlog par dka' / /de ltar ser sna can de la/ /dbang bskur mi bya gzhan po bya/ /cho ga'i rim pa bstan pa ni/ /rgyas par byed na bskyed rim rdzogs par bya/ /yang na bsdus dang shin tu bsdus/ de ltar byas 'og nad pas ni/ /khrus kyi
30a3(rgyud 'grel): rim pa rdzogs byas la/ /gos bzang byin brlabs bskon nas ni/ /shar gyi phyogs su la bltas nas/ /mdun du maN+Dal lnga byas te/ /dang po phyag 'tshal mchod pa 'bul/ /de nas sdigs bshags la sogs bya/ /nad pa de ni mi nus na/ /mchod g.yog dag gi byed du gzhug
30a4(rgyud 'grel): de nas skyabs gsol tshigs bcad brjod/ /bcom ldan rdo rje gos sngon can/ /sku mchog stobs ldan khyod phyag 'tshal/ /gsung mchog sgra mchog 'bar la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thugs mchog ye shes ldan la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sku mchog stobs chen khyod la phyag
30a5(rgyud 'grel): 'tshal lo/ /de nas lus 'bul zhes ni sbyar/ /bdag la gnod pa'i nad rnams kun/ /khyod kyi mthu yi sbyad du gsol/ /'byung po'i gnod pa bzlog tu gsol/ /zor dang dug rnams thams cad kyang/ mthu stobs bdag pos bzlog pa gsol/ /bcom ldan khro chen
30a6(rgyud 'grel): rnam par rgyal/ /sku gsung thugs ldan khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal ldan mgon po nag po che/ /lus ngan rgyal po mthu bo che/ /khro bo chen po bdud rtsi 'khyil/ /rdo rje gnod sbyin 'jigs chen po/ /ro langs ma ni mthu mo che/ /rdo rje mkha' 'gro dpal 'bar ma//

34b5(rgyud 'grel): tshom bu dgram/ /sa la gnas pa'i mkha' 'gro ma/ /bskyod cing spyan drangs bstim byas la/ /byin gyis brlabs la mchod pa bya/ /lhag ma kha chus btab nas ni/ /sbyang dang spro ba bsdu byas la/ /'khor khang phyi logs maN+Dal bya/ /khrag gis byugs shing me
34b6(rgyud 'grel): tog dgram/ /bshug glu brda' yis spyan drangs la/ /rnal 'byor skra bshig thal ba byug /rgyan chas gon la rtags rnams gdab/ /lha yi ting 'dzin gsal byas nas/ /rdo rje'i glu glangs rol mo brdung/ /mchod cing bstod nas mthol bshags bya/ /'phrin las
34b7(rgyud 'grel): bcol la gshegs su gsol/ /byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tshogs kyi sbyor ka'i 'phrin las kyis/ /rnal 'byor pa'i las rnams 'grub/ /slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //zab pa don gyi cho ga rnams/ /rin chen lta bu'i gang
35a1(rgyud 'grel): zag la/ /zab phyir man ngag bkol nas bstan/ mchog gi tshogs kyi 'khor lo ni/ /thun mong cho ga thams cad ni/ /thun mong cho gas 'khor dad mthun no/ /khyad par cho ga bstan pa ni/ /rin chen phug pa dgu rim mam/ bdun rim lnga rim sum rin ni/
35a2(rgyud 'grel): mu stegs nyan thos skyes pa yi/ /skrag 'gyur log sbyod sbyad byed gsum/ /de dag spang phyir gong bzhin bstan/ rgyal rigs rje rigs bram pa'i rigs/ /du mo mtshan dang ldan pa ni/ /mtshan rnams bcu po rdzogs pa dang/ /shes rab che dang snying rje che/ /dad pa la
35a3(rgyud 'grel): sogs che ba dang/ /rnal 'byor ldan zhing phyag rgya mkhas/ /sbyor thabs kun la rab tu mkhas/ /de lta'i rnal 'byor nyung yang lnga/ /mang par gyur na rnal 'byor kyang/ /bskyed de de ltar rig par spyad/ lnga gnyis zung bu gnas pa las/ /bskyed pa'i rim pa mthar
35a4(rgyud 'grel): yin pas/ /nang gi mchod pa brtsam par bya/ /de nas gsang ba'i mchod pa brtsam/ /gsang ba'i mchod pa'i cho ga yis/ /dga' ba'i ye shes bcu drug ni/ /'khor lo'i tshul las lhan cig bskyed/ /ye shes 'khor lo zhes su grags/ /yang na sprul pa'i 'khor
35a5(rgyud 'grel): lo la/ /thig le pa? mo bsam pa ni/ /rnal 'byor pha yin rtsa rnams mo/ /rlung ni las kyi sems pa yis/ /de la sogs pa'i man ngag rnams/ /slob dpon zhal las shes par bya/ /'khor lo gsum la'ang de bzhin no/ /tshogs zhes bya ba mang ba yin/ /
35a6(rgyud 'grel): 'khor lo zhes bya bskor du btub/ /mchog ces bya ba lhan cig gda' / /de ltar mchog gi 'khor lo ni/ /yang yang sbyang zhing bsgom par bya/ /mchog gi tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka ste gnyis pa'o// //dgug pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo ni/ /thun mong
35a7(rgyud 'grel): cho ga thams cad ni/ /thun mong cho gas 'khor dang mthun no/ /khyad par cho ga bstan pa ni/ /dur khrod 'jigs pa'i gnas dag tu/ /shin tu dmar ba'i gos gyon nas/ /nub phyogs su ni kha bltas te/ /cho ga gsum gyis ltar bskyed nas/ /'khor bskyed pa'am mi bskyed
35b1(rgyud 'grel): pa'o/ /bskyed pa hUM gis bskyed pa dang/ /mi bskyed skad cig sprul ba'o/ /ye shes dkyil 'khor spyan drangs sogs/ /byas nas bskyed rim mdza' byin nas/ mdun gyi dkyil 'khor sprul pa la/ /cho ga la sogs rdzogs byas nas/ /dur khrod ras ma dag la ni/ /mdun
35b2(rgyud 'grel): du gzugs pa ma 'khor lo bri/ /dgug pa'i yi ge'i 'od zer gyis/ /bsgrub bya bkug nas bstim par bya/ /'jig rten 'das dang 'jig rten pa'i/ dkyil 'khor bzhi po de dag la/ /mchod bstod? la sogs byas nas ni/ /'phrin las bcol zhing rbad pa dang/ /
35b3(rgyud 'grel): sngags bzlas brgya rtsa brgyad du ni/ /rab gyis bya ba 'bring gi ni/ /lnga brgya tha ma stor gis so/ /bzhi pa rab tu re re yang/ de bzhin cig gis 'grub pa dang/ yang na thun par bzhi dag tu/ /rtsa gcig lnga bcu brgya rtsa brgyad/ /de lta'i 'khor lo rtsa gcig dang
35b4(rgyud 'grel): lnga bcu brgya rtsa brgyad du ni/ /sgrub po khyad par rab 'bring gis/ /bsgrub bya gang yin khugs par bsam/ /nyi shu rtsa drug mdza' las ni/ /bsgrub bya'i ming ni bcug nas su/ 'gugs byed bsre bar gzhug par bya/ /dgug pa tshogs kyi sbyor ka la/ /nyin dang mtshan du
35b5(rgyud 'grel): brtson par bya/ /dgug pa tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka ste gsum pa'o// //bskrad pa tshogs kyi 'khor lo ni/ /thun mong cho ga thams cad ni/ /phan gdags pa ni nyid dang mthun/ /khyad par 'jigs pa'i gnas dag tu/ /lho phyogs su ni kha bltas te/ /sngon
35b6(rgyud 'grel): po la sogs gos gen la/ /bskyed rim tshul du bya ba dang/ /cho ga gsum gyis bya ba yin/ /de nas ye shes spyan drangs nas/ /cho ga la sogs rdzogs par bya/ /mdun du dur khrod ras ma la/ /rlung gi dkyil 'khor bris nas ni/ /de steng zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la/
35b7(rgyud 'grel): bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan bris nas ni/ /rnal 'byor ci 'dod mdun du bsam/ /yang na gtso bo lnga 'am drag po gnyis/ /las la med du mi rung ngo/ gtso bo drag po las ni bsdus/ /slob dpon gnyis po shin tu bsdus/ /dkyil 'khor gsum po sprul pa las
36a1(rgyud 'grel): cho ga la sogs rdzogs par bya/ /cho gas kyi rdzas rnams ma lus bsag /khyad par tsit+ta sna tshogs dang/ /sha sna khrag sna la sogs pa'i/ /tshul khrims bsrung ldan nas bzung nas/ /sgo mangs can ni yan chod kyi/ /rang gi sbyor ba ma byas par//
36a2(rgyud 'grel): gzhan la nyos dang blangs pa yis/ /rdzas rnams rdo rje can gyis ni/ /rgyud las bsngags par bcom ldan gsungs/ /byan pos btse bsred byas nas ni/ /yon bdag 'khor dang bcas pa rnams/ /skor ba bdun nam gsum byas la/ /'gying bag 'dzum pa'i
36a3(rgyud 'grel): mdangs kyis ni/ /slob dpon pa ni rdo rje'i glus/ /phyag rgya brgyud nas drang par bya/ /hUM bla ma rdo rje slob dpon ni/ /gnyis med ye shes mthu ldan pas/ /dbyings las ma g.yos rtogs med kyang/ /sems can gdul ba'i don slad du/ /rdo rje can gyi sku sprul nas/ /rtse
36a4(rgyud 'grel): gcig ldan pa'i ting 'dzin gyis/ /tshogs kyi 'khor lo rgya chen 'di/ /bdag gzhan lha rnams mchod pa yis/ /byin gyis brlabs pa mdzad du gsol/ /de nas rdo rje slob dpon gyis/ /yi ge gsum gyi bdud rtsi yis/ bsreg sbyangs bdud rtsi zhu nas kyang/ /bde gshegs mchod bstod
36a5(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs byas nas/ /'phrin las bcol bas khro bo yi/ /sngags bzlas pas ni bsgrub bya ste/ /'khor lo rlung gi dkyil 'khor la/ /sgrub bya de ru bzhag nas su/ /khro bo dpag med spros pa yis/ /zhal nas rlung nag tshub ma ni/ /btang bas sgrub bya bteg nas
36a6(rgyud 'grel): kyang/ /nub byang mtshams kyis rlung lhas ni/ /khyad par de nyid bskyod nas kyang/ /nam mkha' mthas gtugs sa ru bskyal/ /de ltar lan gsum lha gsum gyis/ /cho ga byas te bskyal bar bya/ /bskrag pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka ste bzhi pa'o// /
36a7(rgyud 'grel): mnan pa tshogs kyi 'khor lo ni/ /thun mong cho ga thams cad ni/ /phan gdags pa ni nyid dang mthun/ /khyad par cho ga bstan pa ni/ /ri bo dben pa'i gnas dag tu/ /slob dpon lho phyogs kha bltas te/ /ser nag la sogs rgyan cha gon/ /cho ga la sogs
36b1(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs byas la/ /rnal 'byor rnams kyi mdun du ni/ /dur khrod ras mdag la ni/ /ba? bla 'am sdong ros khu bas su/ /gser gyi ri rab bris nas kyang/ /de 'og mthing shing dag gis ni/ /rgya mtsho chen po'i gzugs bris la/ /de gnyis dag gi bar du ni/ /bsgrub bya'i ming rnams
36b2(rgyud 'grel): bris nas kyang/ /shugs ldan pa dang mgo 'chas dang/ /kun tu rgyug? pa yan chad kyi/ /sna gsum po ni thams cad kun/ /chos mthun spyod pas btsal nas kyang/ /byan po de rdzogs rjes rnams la/ /yid 'od dpag med bshams nas kyang/ /bskor nas slob dpon la
36b3(rgyud 'grel): phul bas/ cho ga la sogs rdzogs nas ni/ /dkyil 'khor gnyis pa'i cho ga yis/ /sngags bzlas brgya rtsa brgyad pa gnyis/ /ting 'dzin ldan par bsgrub bya ste/ /ming gi yi? bskyed nas kyang/ /yi ge gnyis po'i rab dang/ /rgya mtsho bskyed nas mnan par bya//
36b4(rgyud 'grel): dkyil 'khor mdza' ma'i cho ga las?/ /khar pa'i phyi rol dag tu ni/ /drag? po'i 'grub khung byas nas kyang/ /nag pos kha ni bcad nas kyang/ /de steng las kyi rgya gram bri/ /de sogs cho ga'i sbyor bas su/ /mkha' 'gro rnams kyis mnan
36b5(rgyud 'grel): par bya'o/ /mnan pa'i cho gas kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka ste lnga pa'o// //bsod ba'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo ni/ /thun mong cho ga thams cad ni/ /phan gdags pa dang mthun par bsam/ /khyad par cho ga bstan pa ni/ /dur khrod 'jigs pa'i gnas dag tu/ /slob dpon lho
36b6(rgyud 'grel): phyogs kha bltas te/ /mnan cing drag po rgyan cho gon/ /rnal 'byor rnams kyi mdun du ni/ /dur khrod ras la gzugs bris la/ /phur bu gri gug mtshon cha rnams/ /khro bo'i sngags kyis byin brlabs nas/ /phur bu gdab cing gri yis gtub/ /thun mong rdzas rnams steng du ni//
36b7(rgyud 'grel): gdeng pa can ni sna tshogs kyi/ /gsum dang ldan pa yid du 'ong/ /slob dpon la ni phul nas kyang/ /dang po bsgrub bya de nyid la/ /bkug nas khro bo'i mtshon cha yis/ /bsad pa'i cho ga byas nas su/ /rtsa gcig la sogs sngags kyis ni/ /de bzhi ma byin rlabs byas nas
37a1(rgyud 'grel): su/ /kha po 'khor lo? mchod nas kyang/ /cho ga la sogs rdzogs byas la/ /slar yang bsgrub bya bkug nas ni/ /mdun bsam bsad pa'i sbyor ba yis/ /cho ga rdzogs nas tha ma ni/ /mkha' 'gro ma yis bsad pa yi/ /sbyor bas cho ga rdzogs par bya'o//
37a2(rgyud 'grel): bsad pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo la sbyor ka ste drug pa'o// //bsreg pa'i cho gas kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka ni/ /cho ga thams cad gzhan dang mthun/ /dkyil 'khor gsum du sbyin sreg gsum/ /rnal 'byor ba ni thams cad kyis/ /sngags la sogs pa'i 'khor
37a3(rgyud 'grel): lo yis/ /bskor ba'i chul du phra? ma ni/ /las mkhan gyis ni bsreg par bya'o/ /de yi cho ga thams cad ni/ /sbyin sreg cho gar shes par bya'o/ /bsreg pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka ste bdun pa'o// //btab pa tshogs kyi 'khor lo ni/ /cho ga thams
37a4(rgyud 'grel): cad gzhan dang mthun/ /khyad par cho ga bstan pa ni/ /rnam par bam pa ma yin pa'i/ /mtshan ldan bam chen blangs nas ni/ /ming gi yi ge bskyed nas kyang/ /de nyid dkyil 'khor gsum po la/ /bstab ste yang na rdzas la ni/ /bsams te byin brlabs byas
37a5(rgyud 'grel): nas kyang/ /kar ma dbyug sngon rta mgrin gyis/ /lan gsum lan bdun nyi shu gcig /bstab pa'i tshogs ni mkhas pas so/ /de nas phyi rol dag tu bya/ /de ltar gnyis bstab gsum du bstab/ /slob dpon man ngag shes par bya'o/ /bstab pa tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka ste  
37a6(rgyud 'grel): brgyad pa'o// //thun gsum thun bzhi dag tu ni/ /nyin dang mtshan ni lan gsum du/ /tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka la/ /rnal 'byor can gyis brtson par bya'o/ /dngos grub rnam gnyis 'dod pa dang/ /bar chad rnam gnyis bsal ba'i phyir/ /tshogs kyi 'khor
37a7(rgyud 'grel): lo 'di byas dge bas su/ /thams cad byang chub thob par shog /tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i sbyor ka slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //lots+tsha ba dge slong tshul khrims gzhon nus bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa'o// //
37b1(rgyud 'grel): */ (/lag na rdo rje sbyin sreg gi cho ga bzhugs//) //rgya gar skad du/ hoM tri bi d+hi/ bod skad du/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga /bcom ldan 'das rdo rje can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /sdig pa gzhi la dang bsod nams 'phel/ /dgug dang dbang byed bsad pa'i sa/ /sgrub po rnams la phan btags phyir
37b2(rgyud 'grel): bdag gi sbyin sreg bshad par bya/ /dang po bkra shis gnas dag tu/ /brtag sogs bsdus rgyas rnam gsum bya/ /'bring ni rang nyid gos sngon gyi/ /ting 'dzin ldan pas bka' sgo zhing/ /shar du kha bltas 'byung po la/ /yid dang mthun pa'i gtor ma sbyin/ /yi ge nyi shu rtsa gnyis
37b3(rgyud 'grel): pa 'am/ /hUM gis yang ni sgrub? bar bya/ /rdo rje phyag rgya de bzhin shes/ /snying ga'i yi ges skyon sbyangs shing/ /sngags dang phyag rgyas sbyang ba'o/ /de ni rgyas pa'i rtags sogs 'dod/ /'bring ni sngags dang phyag rgyas sbyang/ /me tog chom bu grangs mnyam pa/ /gzhung bzhin bris pa rdzogs
37b4(rgyud 'grel): bar 'dod/ /mdza' ma mdzes pa'i snod dag la/ /yig 'bru gsum gyis byin brlabs nas/ /ting 'dzin sbyang ba kho nar 'dod/ /sa skyon sbyang ba gsum zhes bya/ /thab brtsig rgyar ni khru gang la/ /zabs su khru phyed blum pos bskor/ /sor bzhi gsum ni dor byas la/ /rdo rje dbus
37b5(rgyud 'grel): su brgyad pa'i tshad/ /thab khung dkar po rgyab tu me ri'o/ /steng du rdo rje phyi rol 'od zer dkar/ /bud shing dkar po khru gang tshad/ /tsanda na dkar po 'o mas spangs te bzhag /mchod sbyin shing ni mdzub gang tshad/ /'dab ma dang bcas rtse mo'i ngos/ /sngar bzhin sbyangs pas yam shing
37b6(rgyud 'grel): bya/ /dkar gsum mngar gsum mar gyi 'og /'bras chan 'bru ni sna tshogs dang/ /ku sha yon chab g.yas su bzhag /me tog la sogs bsang gtor dang/ /zhal bsil rnams ni g.yon du bzhag /dgang gzar dang ni blugs gzar gnyis/ /mtshan nyid rgyas par gzhan du
37b7(rgyud 'grel): bstan/ /yang na g.yas kyi sor mo bskum pa las/ /yi ge hUM gi 'od zer de yis ni/ /rdo rje can gyi 'od zer bkug pa yis/ /rdul shig ye shes gong bu las/ /rdo rje khro bo'i dgang gzar gyur/ /g.yon gyi mthe bos mthe chung mnan/ /gong bzhin sbyangs nas blugs
38a1(rgyud 'grel): gzar gyur/ /de nyid rdo rje dril ni mthun/ /de nas dkar po'i rgyan cha pa'o/ /yid dang mthun pa ku sha'i steng/ /sems ba'i skyil krung shar du bltas/ /thab sogs tsandan chus gtor te/ /bud shing ma nor zlum por brtsig /de nas rgya ni ku sha la/ /oM a mri ta kuN+Da li
38a2(rgyud 'grel): sarba pignAM nI sha ya hUM phaT/ las kyi sngags kyis bsang gtor bya/ /bum sbyangs bskyed dgug bzlas pa yis/ /bya gcig bdun gyi 'od zer dgang/ /thab kyi khor khor yug la/ /ku sha'i rtse mo phyi ru bston/ /de nas lha yi rnal 'byor ni/ /cho ga lnga 'am cho ga gsum/
38a3(rgyud 'grel): skad cig bsdus rgyas shes par bya/ /thab la sogs pa'i man ngag kyang/ /las kyi cho gas su shes par bya/ /de yang slob dpon man ngag gtso/ /bram ze'i khyim mam gtsub shing mis/ /rlang? g.yang kyis spar las kyis bsang/ /sbyang zhing bskyed nas raM dkar pos//
38a4(rgyud 'grel): me lha dkar po drang srong zhi ba'i tshul/ /tshangs pa'i skud pa dkar por ldan/ /phyag nas dgyug pa bzang? phreng dang/ /guN+De skyabs sbyin bsnams pa'o/ /'od 'phros sngar bzhin spyan drangs te/ /oM ba pa ka a ga na ye/ A gats+tsha ya/ A gats+tsha ya ma ma shAn+tidU ru swA hA/ /lcags kyu'i
38a5(rgyud 'grel): phyag rgya bcings te spyan drang ngo/ /bgegs bskrad bstim ste mchod pa dbul/ /rtsa sngags nyid la mchod sngags btags te dbul/ /oM ba pa ka agna ye/ che ge mo shAn ting ku ru swAhA/ zhes sreg rdzas dbul bar bya'o/ /de yi man ngag 'od zer na/ /sum skor  
38a6(rgyud 'grel): du ni bya ba dang/ /nyis skor du ni bya ba dang/ /bdag nyid rab tu shes par bya/ /bzhi skor dag dang slob ma'o/ /'od zer dkar po 'phros pa las/ /thugs dang snying ga rgyud pa dang/ /gsung nas ngag la brgyud pa dang/ /dbu nas mgo la brgyud pa yi/ /lus ngag yid kyi sgrib
38a7(rgyud 'grel): pa sbyang/ /rtsa ba gsum 'dus bskang bar bya/ /spyi gtsug nas brtsams nas ni/ /sdig dang srin bu zad pa'i phyir/ /dmar pos sreg cing dkar pos bkru/ /sgo dgu dag nas bsdu ba dang/ /thams cad kun nas bsdu ba dang/ /snying gar bsdus nas dbyung ba dang/ /
38b1(rgyud 'grel): til gyis gzugs brnyan byas nas ni/ /sdig pa'i gzugs la de gzhug bya/ /rdzas rnams bdud rtsis mchod pas ni/ /de nas sdig pa de bsreg bya/ /yang na rdzas la bstim ste bsreg /nad rnams ni bar byed pa ni/ /nad kyi ming nas smos nas ni/ /gong ma de bzhin bsregs
38b2(rgyud 'grel): pa'am/ /nad kyi ming dang gzugs bris la/ /'od zer dmar pos bsregs nas ni/ /dkar pos sbyang zhing zhi bsams la/ /'byung ba'i dgra rnams de bzhin bsam/ /'byung po kun dang dgra kun yang?/ /'od zer bkye bas zhi bar bsam/ /gzugs dang ming bris zhi bar bya/ /sreg
38b3(rgyud 'grel): rdzas bdud rtsi 'od kyis mchod/ /mchod pas mnyes pas gong bzhin bskor/ /de lta min ni 'og bzhin no/ /man ngag de la nan tan bya/ /mar dang dkar gsum mngar gsum dang/ /yam shing mar 'og chan dang nas/ /de la sogs pa'i thun rdzas rnams/ /rim pa bzhin du  
38b4(rgyud 'grel): dbul bar bya/ /til ni med du mi rung ngo/ /tha ma de gang blugs mthol bshags bya/ /bstod cing phrin las bcol bar bya/ /thugs ka nyid du pho brang bcas/ /skad cig de gsal ye shes dgug /bstim la mchod pa rnam lnga bya/ /rtsa sngags mchod sngags btags te
38b5(rgyud 'grel): dbul/ /sreg rdzas kun kyang de bzhin bya/ /man ngag rim pa 'dir shes bya/ /slob dpon zhal las shes par bya/ /bdun nam nyi shu rtsa gcig gam/ /brgya rtsa brgyad ni bsdus rgyas pa'o/ /rtsa lnga lnga bcu brgya yis ni/ /ji ltar 'dod pa zhi bar 'gyur/ /sdig pa che bar gyur
38b6(rgyud 'grel): nas ni/ /nyis 'gyur gsum ni brgyad brgya'o/ /shin tu che gyur stong gi bar/ /de yi sdig dang bsod nams ni/ /che chung rab 'bring shes par bya'o/ /de ltar byas na nges par zhi/ /tha ma dgang blugs mthol bshags bya/ /bstod cing las bcol gshegs su gsol/ /ting 'dzin
38b7(rgyud 'grel): bsdus nas me lhag mas/ /mchod nas sreg rdzas gong bzhin dbul/ /dgang blugs la sogs rdzogs byas la/ /ting 'dzin bsdus te spyod lam bya/ /thun gsum sbyor ka sbyin sreg la/ /rnal 'byor can gyis brtson par bya/ /sbyin sreg gi spyod ka slob dpon b+ha bas m?
39a1(rgyud 'grel): pa rdzogs so// //rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg bya ba ni/ /maN+Dal kha dog ser po la/ /khru de khru phyed khru gang du/ /bskor te gru bzhi 'am zur brgyad du/ /byas nas sor gnyis sor bzhi can/ /dbus su rin chen 'bar bas mtshan/ /bar du me ri'i kha khyer steng
39a2(rgyud 'grel): rin chen rdo rjes bskor bar bri/ /ser po'i rgyan chas bgos nas ni/ /byang phyogs ngos su kha bltas la/ /bskyed pa'i rim pa'i tshul bsgoms nas/ /las kyi bum pa sbyang sogs bya'o/ /'bras bu 'o ma can gyi shing/ /kha dog ser po dbus kyi cha/ /thab khung dbus
39a3(rgyud 'grel): su bcer bar bya/ /khru gang khru phyed mdzub gang du/ dri zhim spangs pa yam shing bya/ /las kyi bum pas bsangs nas ni/ /mchod rdzas ser po la sogs rnams/ /g.yon du mar sar zhol sogs/ /me sar brtag cing thab khung sbyang/ /thab bskyed me lha bskyed pa
39a4(rgyud 'grel): ni/ /sde chen drug pa'i gsum pa dang/ /gnyis pa lnga yi dang po ni/ /bskyed pa la ni bsngags par gsungs/ /me lha ser po zhal gcig ni/ /phyag bzhi phyag gnyis dbang chen kun/ /spyan drangs bstims te dbang bskur ro/ /mchod pa la sogs byas nas ni/ /de nas
39a5(rgyud 'grel): sreg rdzas rnams ni dbul/ /rtsa sngags nyid la mdza' bzhi ru/ /gzar bu rin chen rdo rjes bya'o/ /rgyas par bstan pa zhe dang mthun/ /man ngag gnyis skor la sogs kyang/ /zhi dang mthun te khyad par ni/ /'od zer sna bug zhugs nas ni/ /snying ga dag tu
39a6(rgyud 'grel): phyin nas ni/ /lus kun rtsa yi rlung rnams dang/ /byang chub sems ni gsal zhing rgyas/ /yang na 'od zer lus kun la/ /khyab pas tshe dang bsod nams dang/ /stobs rnams gang 'dod rgyas par 'gyur/ tha ma dgang blugs bstod par bya/ /de ni 'bar ba'i rnam
39a7(rgyud 'grel): pa 'am/ /thugs ka nyid du gos sngon can/ /bskyed nas spyan drangs bstim byas la/ /dbang bskur mchod pa la sogs bya/ /dgang blugs bstod nas bshags par bya/ /ye shes gshegs nas ting 'dzin bsdu/ /yi ge bcu bdun mdza' bsgyur la/ /
39b1(rgyud 'grel): bdun nam nyi shu rtsa gcig tu/ /brgya rtsa brgyad du bzlas te bya/ /me lha rdzas rnams bsdus nas ni/ /cho ga la sogs gong bzhin bya/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig nas bzung nas/ /stong gi bar du tshun chad du/ /sbyor ba gnyis po gang byas kyang/ /ji ltar 'dod pa rgyas par 'gyur/ thun gsum
39b2(rgyud 'grel): sbyin sreg sbyor ka las/ /rnal 'byor can gyis brtson par bya'o/ /rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg gi sbyor ka ste gnyis pa'o// //slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa rdzogs so// //dbang gi sbyin sreg spyor ka ni/ /sa gzhi dmar ba'i thab khung du/ /b+ha ga lta bu
39b3(rgyud 'grel): 'am zla gam bya/ /tshad ni rgyas pa'i chung 'bring ngo/ /kha khyer mu ran gnyis dang bzhi/ /gri gug gam gzhu ni dbus su mtshan/ /pad+ma dmar po 'dab brgyad la'o/ /bud shing dmar po tsher ma'i shing/ /yam shing sor ni bcu gnyis sam/ /sor brgyad tshad la dri mar
39b4(rgyud 'grel): bsku/ /mchod rdzas dmar po g.yas su bzhag /mar la sogs pa'i bsreg rdzas ni/ /dmar po'i ro dang dris bsgyur nas/ /g.yon du bzhag nas stan dmar po/ /rol pa'i 'dug stangs nub phyogs blta/ /dmar po la sogs rgyan chas pa'o/ /bud shing bcer? te
39b5(rgyud 'grel): bcad par bya/ /bskyed pa'i rim pa tshul bsgoms nas/ /me spar la sogs cho ga bya/ /rlung gi yi ge bsngags pa yin/ /kha dog dmar po rlung la gnas/ /spyan drangs bstims te dbang bskur ro/ /mchod pa la sogs dbul ba ni/ /me lha'i sngags la mdza' bsgyur la/ /cho
39b6(rgyud 'grel): ga la sogs rdzogs nas ni/ /me lha'i thugs kar lha bskyed nas/ /spyan drangs la sogs cho ga bya/ /'od zer dmar po 'phros nas ni/ /lha mnyes pas ni dgug pa'i bsam/ /yang na man ngag sbyor ba gsum/ /tha ma me yi cho ga ni/ /me lha'i sngags kyis gsum mam
39b7(rgyud 'grel): bdun/ /lha ni nyi shu rtsa brgyad bsngags/ /bdun nam brgya yi bar du bya/ /de ltar sbyin sreg sbyor ka la/ /nyin mtshan du ni brtson par bya'o/ /slob dpon b+ha bas mdzad pa dbang gi sbyin sreg gi sbyor ka ste gsum pa rdzogs so// //bsad pa'i sbyin sreg
40a1(rgyud 'grel): sbyor ka ni/ /thab khung gru gsum kha dog gnag /rdo rje gri gug nang dang steng/ /bar du me ri rtse mo 'phags/ /bdud rtsi la sogs tshon rtsi byug /bud shing nag po tsher ma can/ /yam shing de mthun bcu gnyis tshad/ /mchod rdzas la sogs nag po
40a2(rgyud 'grel): shing/ tshil chen mar nag la sogs pa'i/ /khyad par gdong? pa can gyis/ /rgyud las byung ba'i sreg rdzas shis/ /nam phyed nyin phyed dus dag tu/ /sa gzhi mtho ba'i stan dag la/ /brkyang bskum la sogs rgyan cha rdzogs/ /bskyed rim tshul du byas nas ni//
40a3(rgyud 'grel): me spar? la sogs cho ga bya/ /me lha gang 'dod bskyed nas ni/ /ye shes spyan drangs mchod sogs dbul/ /rnal 'byor sbyor ka'i man ngag ni/ /'di ni shin tu zab ces pas/ /gzu lums rtog gi dgag pa'i phyir/ /slob dpon zhal las shes par bya'o/ /lha yi cho
40a4(rgyud 'grel): ga rdzogs nas ni/ /me lha gsang ste ting 'dzin bsdu/ /rdzas rnams thams cad bsdus nas ni/ /cho ga la sogs rdzogs bya'o/ /drag po las kyi sbyor ka ste bzhi pa rdzogs so// //bsdus pa las kyi sbyor ka ni/ /thun mong cho ga thams cad ni/ /gong? 
40a5(rgyud 'grel): bzhin du shes byas la/ /brko zhing bru ba ma nus pas/ /maN+Dal bdud rtsis byugs nas su/ /tshon rnams kyis ni bri bar bya/ /de nas cho ga rdzogs bya'o/ /shin tu bsdus pa'i sbyor ka ni/ /maN+Dal byas la me tog dgram/ /skad cig lhar bskyed byin brlabs
40a6(rgyud 'grel): la/ /bsrung ba'i cho ga byas nas ni/ /cho ga la sogs rdzogs bya'o/ /khyad par zhi ba dag? la ni/ /dngul dang 'khar ba dag ni shis pa ste/ /rgyas pa gser dang ra gan dang/ /dbang ni zabs? la drag po lcags/ /khyi yi thod pa'ang bya par gsungs/ /dbyibs?
40a7(rgyud 'grel): rnams so sor byas pa'am/ /yang na bsams te byas pa'o/ /de rnams rnyed par ma gyur na/ /sa ni rin chen dang 'dra bas/ /kham phor snod rnams kun la ni/ /so so'i dbyibs ni byas pa dang/ /bsams te byin gyis brlabs byas la/ /cho ga la sogs
40b1(rgyud 'grel): rdzogs bya'o/ /sbyin sreg las kyi sbyor ka rnams/ /rna bar brgyud pa'i rim pa yis/ /rgyud la gab pa'i don rnams kun/ /bdag gis sgrub pa po la bstan/ /'di bstan pa yi dge bas ni/ /thams cad byang chub thob par shog /sbyin sreg las kyi cho ga /slob dpon b+ha bas
40b2(rgyud 'grel): mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar skad du/ /badzra pA Ni nI lAM ba ra d+ha ra ho tri bi d+hi/ bod skad du/ phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can gyi sbyin sreg gi cho ga /dpal gos sngon can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /man ngag rim pa dran tsam zhig /slob ma'i don du bshad
40b3(rgyud 'grel): par bya/ /sngon du bsnyen pa rdzogs pa yis/ /sgrub pa yi ni dus dag tu/ /sbyin sreg dag gis bsad par bya/ /sa brtag blang zhing sbyang ba dang/ /byin gyis brlab cing bsrung pa dang/ /snying pa dag tu bya mi dgos/ /maN+Dal sku gsum lho phyogs bstan/ /khru gang tshang la
40b4(rgyud 'grel): byed brkos na/ /gsum dor gsum ni kha khyer ro/ /bdud rtsi la sogs chen rtsis nag por bya/ /de dbus rdo rje steng yang de/ /bar du me ri rtse mo 'phags/ /bud shing gnag cing gdug pa'i shing/ /thab kyi tshad las sor mtho tsam/ /yam shing de mthun bcu gnyis
40b5(rgyud 'grel): tshad/ /mchod rdzas nag po la sogs shis/ /sreg rdzas mar nag rus khrag sha/ ske tshe shangs tshe yungs kar dang/ /de la sogs pa'i mthun rdzas bya/ /rdzas de rnams kyis gzugs brnyan bya/ /mchod rdzas g.yas la sreg rdzas g.yon/ /byin gyis brlab cing
40b6(rgyud 'grel): bzhag par bya/ /dgang gzar blugs gzar gzhan dang mthun/ /yang na leg pa dag gis bya/ /de gnyis rdo rje dril bu yang/ /mdun nyid du yang bzhag par bya/ /las kyi bum pas thams cad bsad?/ /dus ni nam phyed nyi phyed bya/ /rgyan cha gon la lho phyogs blta/ /
40b7(rgyud 'grel): g.yon brkyang 'dug ste drag tu bzlas/ /mche ba gtsigs shing khro gnyer bsdu/ /dang po bskyed pa sngon song nas/ /me sbar brtag cing bgegs bzlog bya/ /bzang na de ni bya mi dgos/ /tha mas sbyang zhing bskyed pa dang/ /cho ga gsum dang skad cig mas/ /me lha nag po khros pa
41a1(rgyud 'grel): bskyed/ /ye shes me lha spyan drangs bstim/ /gnyis su med par rgyas btab la/ me lha'i sngags la mchod sngags btags te dbul/ /de nas sreg rdzas dbul bar bya/ /de dbul ba yi man ngag kyang/ /khro bo dag gi cho 'phrul gyis/ /gzugs
41a2(rgyud 'grel): can dgug bstim btubs te dbul/ /yang na rdzas mchod mnyes pa las/ /'od zer khro bos dgug cing bsreg /man ngag de la nan tan bya/ /oM badzra kro d+ha agne/ che ge mo mA ra ya phaT/ stong rtsa brgyad nas brgya rtsa brgyad/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig bar du'o/ /yang
41a3(rgyud 'grel): na bsod nams dag gi rim pa yis/ /brgya dang stong dang khri ru bya/ /de ltar byas pas nges gsod cing/ /khyad par du ni 'byung po gsed/ /tha ma dbang phyugs bstod bya'o/ /de yi thugs kar gos sngon bskyed/ /ye shes sems dpa' spyan drangs bstim/ /rgyas
41a4(rgyud 'grel): btab mchod pa gong bzhin dbul/ /de nas sreg rdzas rim bzhin dbul/ /rtsa sngags nyid kyis dbul bar bya/ /gong gi man ngag shes par bya/ /dbang blugs phul la bstod par bya/ phrin las bcol zhing gshegs su gsol/ /ting 'dzin bsdus te me
41a5(rgyud 'grel): lha bsam/ /rdzas rnams thams cad bsdus nas ni/ /me yi lha la dbul zhing bstod pa bya/ /'phrin las bcol zhing gshegs su gsol/ /ting 'dzin bsdus te spyod lam bya/ /slob ma rnams kyi don ched du/ /bdag gis man ngag 'di bkod

41a7(rgyud 'grel): bla ma gus pa 'ang dpag tu med/ /de 'dra'i sems can dpag med kyang/ /bsdus nas gsum du 'dus 'gyur te/ /sprul dang kha dog rjes 'jug pa'o/ /rjes 'jug gnyis su shes par bya'o/ /sprul la mthun 'jug sbyang ba med/ /sprul rjes
41b1(rgyud 'grel): 'jug gi gang zag la/ /dam tshig nyams pa mang 'byung yang/ /nyams pa rnam pa gsum du 'dus/ /lus ngag yid du shes par bya/ /lus kyi dam tshig nyams pa ni/ /sA ts+tshas sbyongs te tshogs sbyor ltos/ /ngag gi nyams pa bzlas pas bdag /yid kyi
41b2(rgyud 'grel): lha yi sbyor kar ltos/ /thun mong sbyin sreg tshogs gtor rnams/ /phan 'dogs sbyor kar blta bar gyis/ /nus pa chung pa'i rnal 'byor bas/ /me bshags maN+Dal gyis sbyang bya/ /maN+Dal bsdu ni rnam gnyis te/ /yid kyis bsams dang dngos byed
41b3(rgyud 'grel): pa'o/ /dngos byed skyon spangs gnyen gzhi la/ /brgya 'am lnga bcu nyi shu lnga/ /lnga 'am bsdus pa gcig kyang bya/ /dbyibs legs mdzes pa bsham par bya/ /kha dog kun nas sngo yang rung/ /dkar po mthing kha ser dmar bya/ /yang na yid dang mthun pa'ang rung/ /tshad ni
41b4(rgyud 'grel): khru gang yan chad bya/ /tshan ni dkar rtsi yud ba dang/ /sngo rtsi gur gum mtshal gyis bya/ /ba yi rnam lnga bdud rtsi lnga/ /dum bu gcig par bzhag nas kyang/ /dri zhim pa yi sman gyis bsgo/ /bdud rtsi lnga dang thun mong rdzas/ /gser sogs kha brgyan lnga ldan du//
41b5(rgyud 'grel): bcug la byin rlabs tshul bzhin bya/ /rang nyid cho ga gsum gyis bskyed/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil pa'i sngags 'dis gdab/ /oM a mri ta kuN Da li hUM phaT/ /byin rlabs bkra shis rdzas dang sreg /de yis thams cad bsang bar bya/ /oM a mri ta kuN+Da li ha na ha na hUM
41b6(rgyud 'grel): phaT/ /yungs kar la gdab 'byung po bsreg /rang gi snying ga'i yig 'bru las/ /'od 'phros yi ge a ru gyur/ /de 'phros taM gi yi ge las/ /sa gzhi rin chen bzhi ru gyur/ /sngags 'di btab pas bzlas par 'gyur/ /oM A tsan+d+ra maN+Da la hUM/ /grangs nyi shu rtsa
41b7(rgyud 'grel): gcig tu bzlas/ /oM ratna traM maN+Da la hUM/ tsandan ga pur gla rtsis sogs/ /mdzes pa'i snod du bzhag pa la/ /'od 'phros pas ni du yig thim/ /bdug pa'i mchog tu gyur par bsam/ /rnal 'byor 'byor pa chur gyur yang/ /tsandan med du mi rung ngo/ /rgyan gyi
42a1(rgyud 'grel): me tog lnga gsum sogs/ /gcig sogs yang na lnga grangs bstun/ /de steng pa las pad+mar bya/ /sngags 'dis bdag po'i rkyen pa'o/ /oM pad+ma maN+Da la hUM/ stong ldan 'bum ldan du gyur bsam/ /de'i steng du b+h+ruM yig las/ /gzhal yas khang ni

42b1(rgyud 'grel): nyams pa rnam gsum sbyor/ /suM brgya nyis brgya lnga bcu dang/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas pas ni/ /yan lag che chung nyams pa sbyor/ /de 'o gzhi ba'i sbyin sreg bya/ /nus pa yod na tshogs 'khor bya/ /de 'og bum pa rnams bsams te/ /gcig tu lha mo rnams bskyed de/ /cig tu nor 'dzin mi

62b2(rgyud 'grel): mo brdab cing/ nad dang gdon bgegs thams cad brlag par bsam mo/ /yang yang lcags kyu'i phyag rgya bcas te gong gi mi la bstim mo/ /de nas phur pa gdab cing brub par bya'o/ /e'i tshogs kyis rim pa dang/ /dang po bdag rnal 'byor pa'i mdun
62b3(rgyud 'grel): du mdzub gang ba'i 'brub khung gru gsum brus te/ de'i nang du ming byad bu la bris la gzhag /de'i kha ru g.yam pa sngon po cig la yung ba ser pos ri rab rdo rje rgya gram gyi gzugs bris la gzhag /ma grub byas na bltas ngan 'byung/ /kun la yong na ngo
62b4(rgyud 'grel): mtshar chung/ /lce dbab pa'i bya thabs rdzogs so// //rten 'brel gyi mthus bsrung ba'i thabs ni/ rma bya'i mkhris pa dang/ ka ra bsre la bsku/ sa'i bdud rtsi lo lnga brgya lon pa yan chad bsku'o/ /spos gu gul nag po dang/ gla rtsi dang/
62b5(rgyud 'grel): mu zi dang/ ldong ros dang/ dri chen dang/ cha mnyam du sbyar te/ sbrang rtsis sbrus te dung pa btang ngo/ /sman gyi nus pa ni 'bras bu gsum dang/ bu skyes ma thag pa'i rang 'gyur dang bsres te/ dri chus sbrus pa'i ri lu khar gzhug go /sman gyis
62b6(rgyud 'grel): mchog gis bsrung ba ni/ /a ru ra rnam par rgyal ba bcangs pas bsrung ba'o/ /sa bdag gi nad thub bo// //nyi ma sa bla na la/ sogs pa la 'di gdags so/ /shig byer nan/ mgo nan/ ha na ha na mA ra ya rbad nan/ zhes bzlas shing
62b7(rgyud 'grel): srung ba bya'o/ /rten 'brel gyis mthus bsrung ba rdzogs so// (lag na rdo rje lce dbab kyi sngon 'gro'i sa nag sbyor spyod lam brgyad pa bzhugs//) //bcom ldan 'das phyag na rdo rje gos sngon po can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnal 'byor
63a1(rgyud 'grel): pa rnams rgyun tu bya ba'i cho ga ni/ thun mong gi spyod laM brgyad kyis bstan te/ khrus dang/ mchod pa'i rnal 'byor dang/ zas dang/ skom dang/ gtor ma dang/ sgom pa bzlas brjod kyi spyod lam brgyad do/ /dang po khrus kyis rnal 'byor ni//
63a2(rgyud 'grel): rang nyid bskyed pa'i rim pa sgoms te/ rin chen bum pa mdzes pa ru/ /chu gtsang srog chags med pa dang/ /tsandan la sogs dris su dgang/ /bdag gi thugs ka'i sa bon gyis/ /bum pa sbyangs te b+h+ruM gyis bskyed/ /de ru lha bskyed ye shes bstim/
63a3(rgyud 'grel): mchod byas sngags ni bzlas nas su/ /drangs ni thim nas 'od du zhu/ /rang gi thugs ka'i sa bon gyis/ /yi ge baM bsgom pad+mar gyur/ /de nyid nam mkha' i steng phyogs bsam/ /de steng sangs rgyas spyan la sogs/ /rdzus skyes bum pa thogs pa bsam/  
63a4(rgyud 'grel): rang bzhin dkyil 'khor lha mo yang/ /bdud rtsi bum pa thogs nas su/ /bkra shis rdo rje glu len cing/ /bdud rtsi dkar po dri med kyis/ /rang gi spyi bor blugs par bsam/ /dri med dag nas mi bskyod 'gyur/ /de ni dus chen khyad par du/ /rgyun tu
63a5(rgyud 'grel): 'grub na bsod nams che/ /de ni khrus kyi rnal 'byor rgyas pa'o/ /de nas bsdus pa 'dod pa la/ /rang nyid stong pa'i ngang las ni/ /sa bon las ni lhar bskyed de/ /khrus kyi bum pa dag la yang/ /sngags btab sbyangs te bdud rtsir gyur/ /thugs

63a7(rgyud 'grel): chu la phog pas bdud rtsir gyur/ /lha mo bum pa thogs pa yis/ /khrus byas dri ma dag par 'gyur/ /de dag kun gyi sngon du ni/ /sems bskyed pa dang ldan byas te/ /bdag dang sems can thams cad kun/ /phyag rgya'i dngos grub thob bya'i
63b1(rgyud 'grel): phyir/ /bdag gis khrus ni 'di bya'o/ /mthar smon pa yi byang chub sems/ /phyag rgya'i mchog tu bsngo bar bya'o/ /de rnams sngags dang phyag rgya ni/ /oM badzra Sh+na hUM phaT/ phyag rgya rdo rje khu tshur gnyis mthe bong sbreng ste spyi bor bzhag /yang na rgyud gzhan so so yi//
63b2(rgyud 'grel): sngags dang phyag rgya dag gis bya/ /dbang bskur khrus dang ldan pa yi/ /de nas mchod pa'i rnal 'byor bstan/ /sa gzhi skyon spangs yon tan ldan/ /ba yi rnam lngar ldan pa yis/ /maN+Dal yid 'ong mdzes par byas/ /tshad ldan dbyibs ldan de la ni/ /
63b3(rgyud 'grel): dang por dri ldan chu yis ni/ /byugs che nyi zla'i gdan du bsam/ /de steng me tog 'grems pa'i tshe/ /pad+ma dag tu gyur par bsam/ /de gsum sngags dang brjod par bya/ /mchod pa dri med bshams nas kyang/ /rang nyid cho gas lhar bskyed de/ /rang gi thugs kyi
63b4(rgyud 'grel): sa bon gyis/ /'od 'phros thugs ka'i lha yang gsal/ /pad+ma'i steng du gzugs brnyan shar/ /de nas sngags dang phyag rgya dang/ /ting 'dzin ldan pa'i 'od zer gyis/ /ye shes lha ni spyan drangs te/ /gzugs brnyan nyid la bstim par bya/ /yang na 'od zer
63b5(rgyud 'grel): 'phros pas su/ /bla ma spyan drangs sgrib pa sbyang/ /mi bskyod gyur nas dbu la bzhugs/ /dang po phyag ni btsal bya ste/ /de nas mchod ba rgyas par dbul/ /de yang dang po bla ma la/ /de nas dkyil 'khor lha la dbul/ /mchod pa dbul ba'i dbul sa

63b7(rgyud 'grel): bya/ /bdug spos shangs la dbul bar bya/ /me tog dbu la dbul bar bya/ lha bshos ljags la dbul bar bya/ /sil snyan snyan la dbul bar bya/ /rin chen mdzod pur dbul bar bya/ /gdugs dang rgyal mtshan la sogs pa/ /sku nyid la ni
64a1(rgyud 'grel): dbul bar bya/ /de ni phyi yi mchod pa dang/ /nang gi mchod pa 'di lta ste/ /sgeg mo la sogs lha mo rnams/ /sbrul la mchod pa dbul bar bya/ /gsang ba'i mchod pa bdud rtsi yis/ /lha rnams dgyes pa bskyed par bsam/ /de 'og rtsa
64a2(rgyud 'grel): ba'i ltung ba rnams/ /rang gi blo la bgrang bsngo bya/ /nyes pa gang gyur de la ni/ /chod du gtad de bshags pa bya/ /dang por bsam pa gtsor byas te/ /tshig gis kyang ni bshags pa bya/ /de 'og yi ge brgya pas skyangs/ /de nas 'jig rten 'das pa dang//
64a3(rgyud 'grel): 'jig rten pa yi dge ba la/ /dga' ba bskyed de rjes yi rang/ /de 'og bla ma dkyil 'khor dang/ /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' la/ /mya ngan mi 'da' gsol ba gdab/ /de nas chos kyi 'khor lo ni/ /bskor ba yang ni gsol ba gdab/ /de
64a4(rgyud 'grel): nas bla ma sangs rgyas dang/ /byang chub sems dpa' dag la yang/ /skyabs su mchi zhing lus kyang dbul/ de 'og sdom pa bzung bar bya/ /rol mo sil snyan ldan pa yis/ /rdo rje sngags ni mgur bcas nas/ /nyi shu rtsa gcig bdun gsum gyis//
64a5(rgyud 'grel): lha rnams la ni bskor ba bya/ /de 'og mchod sogs dge ba rnams/ /byang chub chen por bsngo bar bya/ /ye shes gshegs nas ting 'dzin bsdu/ /de nas ci bder don gzhan bya/ /de ni mchod pa rgyas pa'i tshad/ /de la bsdus pa 'dod pa rnams/ /maN+Dal
64a6(rgyud 'grel): dngos sam yid kyi bsam/ /rang nyid stong pa'i ngang las ni/ /sa bon las ni lhar bskyed de/ /ye shes dkyil 'khor spyan drangs te/ /rdzas rnams dngos su ma 'byor yang/ /sngags dang phyag rgya ting 'dzin gyis/ /mchod pa rnam lnga gsang
64a7(rgyud 'grel): mchod tsam/ /yid kyis bshags pa la sogs bya/ /shin tu bsdus par 'dod pa la/ /rang nyid skad cig lhar bsams te/ /bla ma yi dam lha la sogs/ /rdzus skyes tshul du mdun du bsam/ /bsam pas bdud rtsi mchod pa dang/ /sdig pa
64b1(rgyud 'grel): bshags dang dge rtsa bsngo/ /'di ni shin tu bsdus pa'o/ /zas kyi rnal 'byor bstan pa ni/ /rang nyid cho gas lhar bskyed la/ /lte ba'i 'og tu rlung bsams te/ /de steng 'byung ba me bsam mo/ /rlung gi me lces snying ga slebs/ /snying ga'i dkyil 'khor la gsal

64b3(rgyud 'grel): snod ni a las ka pA la/ /rdzas ni bdud rtsi'i yi ge yis/ /bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga ru bsam/ /de 'og raM dang yaM las ni/ /me dang rlung gi dkyil 'khor ni/ /gru gsum zla gam ba dan can/ /thod pa'i nang gi yi ge gsum/ /mu tig tsang la
64b4(rgyud 'grel): brgyus pa bzhin/ /de steng rdo rje lte ba la/ /yi ge hUM gis mtshan par bsam/ /de steng zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la/ /yi ge oM gyis mtshan pa bsam/ /yi ge hUM gi 'od zer gyis/ /ba dan bskyod pas rlung byung ste/ /rlung gi ma spang bdud rtsi
64b5(rgyud 'grel): bzhu/ /hUM gis bsdus shing A(rgyud 'grel): su zhu/ /oM gyis kha dog dkar por bsgyur/ /slar yang gyen du spros pas su/ /steng gi oM bskul 'od zer 'phros/ /rang bzhin lha yi mdzod spur phog /gnyis med rol pas byang sems phab/ /dang por oM
64b6(rgyud 'grel): phog zla ba zhu/ /dam tshig dang 'dres rdo rje phab/ /cha gnyis gcig 'dres rdo rjer zhu/ /bdud rtsi dri med dkar po des/ /snying ga'i lha la mchod byas te/ /sbyin sreg tshul du bza' bar bya/ /zas kyi rnal 'byor rgyas pa'o/ /rang nyid lhag pa'i lhar
64b7(rgyud 'grel): bsams te/ /snying khar lha yi rnal 'byor bsam/ /zas rnams byin gyis brlab pa ni/ /pad+ma mdzes pa'i snod ngag tu/ /bdud rtsi rnam pa lnga bsams te/ /lag pa g.yon pa'i zla steng nas/ /oM las 'od 'phros bdud rtsi bsregs/ g.yas kyi
65a1(rgyud 'grel): nyi ma'i steng nas ni/ /A(rgyud 'grel): yis 'od 'phros bdud rtsi spel/ /gnyis ka las ni hUM 'phros te/ /bdud rtsi rnams ni 'od du 'bar/ /ho las 'od 'phros bdud rtsi bzhu/ /de nas thugs ka'i lha mchod do/ /de nas bsdus pa'i

65b1(rgyud 'grel): mchod pa ni/ /phyi rol maN+Dal stong steng du/ /chos 'byung gru gsum bri bar bya/ /me tog tshom bu dgod par bya/ /rdzogs pa'i rnal 'byor ting 'dzin gyis/ /ye shes dkyil 'khor spyan drangs te/ /pad+ma'i steng du bzhugs bsams la/ /so so'i rtsa ba'i sngags

66a1(rgyud 'grel): rang yi dam lhar bsams te/ /'gro ba pho rnams thams cad ni/ /bde gshegs sprul pa nyid du bltas/ /'gro ba mo rnams thams cad ni/ /bde gshegs yul gyi lha mor blta/ /snod kyi 'jig rten 'di dag kun/ /lha

66a7(rgyud 'grel): blang/ /sgom pa bstan pa'i rim pa yang/ /bla ma 'chad pa'i brgyud shes pas/ /slob ma nyid kyis shes par bya/ /rin chen lta bu'i gang zag la/ /rdzogs pa'i man ngag rim pa bstan/ /de las gzhan pa'i slob ma la/ /bskyed pa'i rim

66b5(rgyud 'grel): nan tan cher bskyed cing/ /phyag na rdo rje lce dbab kyi sngon du 'gro ba'i yan lag /rnal 'byor gyi spyod lam brgyad pa zhes bya ba/ /slob dpon rgyal pu sprin gyi shugs can gyis mdzad pa rdzogs so// //slob dpon rgyal bu sprin gyi

67a1(rgyud 'grel): pa'i sa bon gyis gos sngon po can dang/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' la sogs pa spyan drangs te/ sa bon las byung ba'i mchod pas mchod do/ /de nas 'di skad du/ dpal phyag na rdo rje dang/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub
67a2(rgyud 'grel): sems dpa' la sogs pa phyogs bcu na bzhugs so 'tshal la/ bdag lus ngag yid gsum gyi sgo nas phyag 'tshal zhing skyabs su gsol lo/ /mchod pa bla na med pa 'dod pa'i yon tan gyi char dag pa'i sems kyis sprul zhing mchis

67a4(rgyud 'grel): bzhugs pa rnams la/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskul bar bgyi'o/ /bde bar gshegs pa gang dag mya ngan 'da' bar bzhed pa rnams la 'khor ba ji srid par gsol ba 'debs so/ /dge ba'i rtsa ba de dag thams cad kyang bla na med pa'i

95b3(rgyud 'grel): bsal bar bya/ /sman ldan gser gyi thur ma yis/ /ye shes dag par mig 'byed do/ /oM badzra na tra a pa ha ra pa Ta li h+ri/ de nas me long g.ya' dag bstan/ /chos rnams gzugs brnyan lta bus te/ /ngag cing gsal la rnyog pa med/ /brjod du med
95b4(rgyud 'grel): cing gzung du med/ /rgyu dang las las thams cad 'byung/ /de nas rdo rje me long phyar/ /rdo rje sems dpa' me long ltar/ /dag cing gsal la dri ma med/ /sangs rgyas kun bdag rang bzhin ni/ /bu khyod kyi ni snying la gnas/ /zhes bya to yis mda' gzhu
95b5(rgyud 'grel): sbyin/ /bskyod la phyogs bzhir bdud la 'phang/ /de nas hUM las skyes pa yis/ /'khor lo rkang pa'i bar bcug la/ /de ring phan chad 'jig rten la/ /skyob pa rnams kyi 'khor lo bskor/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bla na med/ /kun tu dri ma sdig dang bral//
95b6(rgyud 'grel): de nas dung byin bus nas kyang/ /chos kyi dung ni bla na med/ /som gnyi yid gnyis mi bya zhing/ /dogs pa med pa'i sems kyis su/ /sangs rgyas spyod pa'i tshul gyis mchog /'jig rten 'dir ni rab tu sgrogs/ /de ltar byas na sangs rgyas la/ /phan btags
95b7(rgyud 'grel): drin du gzo zhes bya/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa 'di kun kyang/ /khyod ni rjes su bsrung bar byed/ /de nas rigs lngar bsam byas la/ /'jig rten khams ni ma lus par/ /sems can ma lus drang ba'i phyir/ /chags pa med pa'i bsam pa yis/ /ji ltar gdul bya sna tshogs
96a1(rgyud 'grel): pa'i/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar gyis/ /de bzhin rigs kyis gang 'dul ba/ /khyod kyi phrin las mchog yin no/ /de nas slar yang rdo rje 'dzin/ /gsal bar byas te tshig 'di brjod/ /de nas bzung nas rigs kyi bus/ /zhi rgyas dbang dang
96a2(rgyud 'grel): bsad pa dang/ /dgug dang bcing dang sreg pa dang/ /bskrad dang dbye ba la sogs pa'i/ /phrin las sna tshogs bsgrub par gyis/ /ral gri mig sman sa 'og dang/ /mchin lham de bzhin ru lu ste/ /thun mong dngos grub ma lus pa/ /de dag khyod kyis bsgrub
96a3(rgyud 'grel): par gyis/ /ma lus snang ba byin par bya/ /bde bar dbugs dbyung rnams kyang sbyin/ /khyad par bkra shis dbang rnams dang/ /rim pa bzhin du rdzogs par bya/ /gal te gsang ba'i dbang bskur ba/ /bzhin bzang mig yangs lang tshor ldan/ /lus la

96a5(rgyud 'grel): mongs 'joms/ /mtshan ldan bde ba bskyed pa de/ /yol bas bar bcad snyoms 'jug brtsam/ /bsrub dang bsrub pa'i sbyor ba yis/ /sgra yi rgyun med longs spyod kyis/ /brlabs kyi rgyun ni chad pa las/ /lhan che skyes pa ye shes kyang/ /rgyun

96a7(rgyud 'grel): bskur nas/ /tshogs dan mchod pa rgya chen bya/ /slob ma dang ldan mchog des kyang/ /rta dang glang po ma he dang/ /bu dang chung ma srog dang dbyig/ ci yod phyag byas ma zhen pas/ /bla ma mnyes phyir dbul bar bya/ /bla mas slob ma dam pa'i mdor/ /bkra shis
96b1(rgyud 'grel): brjod cing gdugs phug pas/ /slob ma mchod pa rdzas thogs nas/ /drin lan dkyil 'khor lan gsum bskor/ /smon lam gdab cing dge ba bsngo/ /tho rangs tshon bsdus bum par blug /chu 'am ri 'am nags phug sba/ /dri bzangs kyis ni thig phyis la/ /
96b2(rgyud 'grel): sa der zhi ba'i me las bya/ /yang na 'phongs pa tshim pa dang/ /tse ta'i las la brtson par bya/ /ji ltar rgyud las gsal gyur cing/ /bla ma'i man ngag thob gyur kyang/ /cung zad spros phyir bdag nyid spro bar byas/ /'on kyang nyes tshogs ci mchis bshags

96b4(rgyud 'grel): slob dpon las kyi rdo rjes mdzad pa rdzogs so// //rgya gar gyi paN+Di ta zla ba bzang po dang/ bod kyi lots+tsha ba glan chung dar ma tshul khrims kyis bsgyur ba'o// (//gos sngon can gyi rgyud kyi rnam bshad dge slong klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa bzhugs/)

96b6(rgyud 'grel): bden pa gnyis la rang gnas shing/ /thabs dang shes rab zung 'brel ba'i/ /mgon po sgrib pa kun spangs yon tan ma lus kun gyi bdag po de/ /shes rab thabs kyis mya ngan mdza' spangs na/ /snying rje chen pos sems can mun 'thibs
96b7(rgyud 'grel): pa/ /mun ma mthong sgom rtsa ba nyon mongs zhi mdzad pa/ /gsang sngags sdud mdzad mi g.yo bcom ldan 'das/ /thugs rje bsnyel ba med la phyag 'tshal lo/ /gang gis gsal bar byas pa de rnams byas pa ma yin tshig don skyon dang ldan/ /de na 'dir

97a2(rgyud 'grel): ni gsal bar byas/ /des ni nyi zla dag dang mthun pa'i bstan bcos 'di/ /thugs rje nye bar bsngos pa yis/ /snying rje ldan pa'i sems kyi su/ /rtsa brgyud man ngag bshad par bya/ /rtsa brgyud rang bzhin don rnams la/ /sde tshan lnga lnga nyi shu lnga/ /yA sha
97a3(rgyud 'grel): mdza' bcas rtsa ba ldan/ /thabs dang shes rab yi ge gnyis ldan gsum du 'dus/ /brjod pa rdzogs byed tshig gi don/ /rtsa ba bshad dang tshig gi don phyi ma/ /phyi ma mchog dang ma log bzhi ru ston/ /bcom ldan rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ /
97a4(rgyud 'grel): 'og min chos dbyings pho brang du/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas der sangs rgyas/ /sprul pa po ni 'dir sangs rgyas/ /ma lus pa yi stobs kyis su/ /sku de rnam pa gsum gyi don/ /thob byed rgyu 'bras gnyis kyi lam/ /dngos byed 'bras bu'i lam
97a5(rgyud 'grel): yin te/ /rgyu ni tshogs te dran sogs pa'i/ /phyi zhing dro ba'i rang bzhin te/ /nyon mongs dam tshig zhi rtse mo'o/ /phyir mi ldog dang 'jig rten mthar stobs lnga/ /dbang po lnga yi rang bzhin no/ /byang chub yan lag bdun po ni/ /mthong lam skad cig bcu
97a6(rgyud 'grel): drug go /sa dang bsgom lam mthar phyin 'bras bu'o/ /dngos byed lam ni 'bras bu sngags/ /byin gyis brlabs sngags mthu yon tan no/ /lam ma bgrod pas 'bras bu med/ /dper na gru gzing bskyod pa yis/ /rin chen mchog ni thob par 'gyur/ /
97a7(rgyud 'grel): brjod bya ston pa'i tshig gis kyang/ /'bras bu bden pa myur du 'byin/ /des na sngags ni gsang sngags lam/ /lam ma bgrod par gsal byed 'gyur/ /des na brjod la khyad kyi nus pa yin no/ /'di skad la sogs pa bshad pa mdzes pa bya ba'i phyir/ /
97b1(rgyud 'grel): rgyud? 'di dang brjod bya ba dang/ /dgos pa dang 'brel pa dang/ /mchog gi dgos pa bstan par bya ste/ brjod bya dngos po med pa'i tshig ni/ /bstan kyang rtogs pa sngon du gtod ba rnams 'jug par mi 'gyur te/ /dung la dkar po spyi ni 'jug gi spyi bye brag la
97b2(rgyud 'grel): 'khrul pa bzhin no/ /des na skyon yod pa'i phyir chos kyis rjes su 'brang ba rnams mi 'jug go /des na byis pa dang smyon pa dang mchog yin zhing gzhan la sogs pa ni dgos pa med snyam pa'am/ /'di nyid kyi ma yin snyam pas mi 'jug ste/ tshig dang don
97b3(rgyud 'grel): thams cad kyi 'brel pa dang/ brjod bya dang/ dgos pa dang/ dgos pa yang dgos pa rnams gtan la phab pa sngon du byas nas mchod pas na/ /'di nyid 'brel pa la sogs pa yang brjod par bya'o/ /de bzhin du 'brel pa dang brjod pa bshad par cis
97b4(rgyud 'grel): te mi bya/ smyon pa'i tshig bzhin du mi 'brel pa'am/ mo sham la sogs pa la don med par/ 'dod pa'i zhen pas tshig chad par 'gyur bas ma ning gi gzugs la zhen pa'i 'dod pa rnams ci nas kyang tshig chad par 'gyur zhes brtags nas 'jug
97b5(rgyud 'grel): par mi 'gyur ba nyid do/ /de bas na 'jug pa'i yan lag gi gtso bo yin pa'i phyir te/ thog ma nyid du dgos pa brjod par bya'o/ /de gang las shes par bya ba'i phyir/ dgos pa dang 'brel pa brjod par bya ba yang bstan to/ /de nas dgos pa'i dgos pa la sogs
97b6(rgyud 'grel): pa bstan to/ /brjod bya ji lta bu snyam pa la/ 'di ltar lam dang 'bras bu brjod bya'i 'bras bur rtog ces bya'o/ /brjod bya ni gnyis su med pa'i ye shes so/ /de yang sgras drangs nas blo la dngos su snang bas/ dngos kyi brjod bya zhes nas snang
97b7(rgyud 'grel): ba zhen pa'i brjod byas/ /sgra drangs pa'i tshig gi don 'dis brjod bya rtogs pas brjod bya/ mtshon par byed pa'i tshig la yang brjod bya 'di yi don zhes 'bral par bya ste/ 'di ltar lam la rten pas 'bras bu thob ste/ /de ni de dang 'gal ba'i chos spro?
98a1(rgyud 'grel): bar 'gyur ro/ /gal te de ltar yin du zad mod/ de nyin bstan pa ci phyir snyam nas des na 'dir sgra'i tshogs la ma rten par nam yang rtogs pa mi 'byung ngo/ /ci'i phyir gal te byung na ni thams cad gzhung gi tshogs la sogs pa mi
98a2(rgyud 'grel): bltos par 'gyur na ni don med do/ /gal te yod na thams cad skye ba 'am/ rkyen med pa rtogs pa thar par gyur pa las/ rgyu med 'bras bu skye bar rigs pa med pa de/ nam mkha' i me tog bzhin no/ /des na rgyu la rang bzhin du bye brag gyur pa med pas rgyu
98a3(rgyud 'grel): med pa las 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /phyi ma lta na yang 'ba' zhig pa rnams la ni 'ba' zhig rang las gzhan nus pa'i phyir mi 'byung ngo/ /'bras bu yan lag rgyu la ma tshang bar byung na ni/ dus thams cad du 'bras bu 'byung ste/ de ni med pa'i phyir ro/ /de
98a4(rgyud 'grel): bas na gzhung gi tshogs med na brjod bya'i rtogs pa mi 'byung ngo/ /de bzhin du gzhung thabs yin pa dang gzhung yang brjod bya'i don rtogs pa thabs dang thabs las 'byung ba'i 'brel pa'o/ /de bas na gzhung gi tshogs 'di brjod bya shugs kyi rtogs bya

98b1(rgyud 'grel): na dgos pa'i dgos pa yang/ gzhan la brten gzhan du mu stegs dang/ nyan thos dang/ rang sangs rgyas dang/ byang chub sems dpa' dang/ phyag rgya chen pos gzhan mthar phyin pa la sogs pa ni/ dgos pa'i dgos pa'o/ /des na chos kyi rjes su 'brang ba rnams la

98b3(rgyud 'grel): nges par bzung nas/ sangs rgyas kyi bka' nges par 'jug pa'i phyir bstan mi dgos so/ /de ltar brjod bya dang dgos pa brjod nas/ lan lag bstan pa ni gzhung don no/ /de la 'di skad bdag gis thos pa zhes pa la sogs pa smos te/ sdud pa po'i tshig tu smos te/
98b4(rgyud 'grel): 'di skad smras pa thos zhes sbyar ro/ /'di'i tshe 'di thos gzhan gyi tshe gzhan gyis thos par bstan to/ /thos pa ni bdag kho nas thos te/ gzhan dang 'brel pa med de/ de ni gzhan thos pa'o/ /'di ni ri rab rtse rtsa rgyud nyi khri sum stong kha nas thos pa'o/ /des ni thos
98b5(rgyud 'grel): pa dka' ba dang/ thos pa mang ba la sogs pa yang yongs su bzung ngo/ /gzhan ni wa ra NA ser bden pa bzhi la sogs pa ste/ gzhan nye bar 'khor dang/ shA ri'i bu la sogs pa'o/ /gtso 'khor tha dad pa'i phyir ro/ /'di skad bdag gis thos ni rgyal ba mar me
98b6(rgyud 'grel): mdzad dang/ shAkya thub pa dang/ gtso bo rdo rje 'chang dang/ rnam rgyal la sogs pas thos pa ste/ sngon dang da lta la sogs pa ste/ bar du yang thos pa ste/ gtso bo 'khor tha mi dad par bstan to/ /tha mi dad na rang gi tshig dang 'gal lo/ /gcig pa yin
98b7(rgyud 'grel): pa'i phyir snyam pa la/ gcig kyang mi stong ste/ kun rdzob tu snang ba thams cad kyang/ 'khrul pa mi bden pa sgyu ma yin pas don ni stong pa nyid kho na'o zhes rgyud las gsungs pa yin no/ /tha dad kyang mi 'gal bde bar gshegs pa la skyon gnyis med de/
99a1(rgyud 'grel): thams cad zhi ba mya ngan las 'das pa khams dang skye mched bral bas dus thams cad bdag dang bdag gis stong pa gnyis su med/ zla ba dang chu bzhin no/ /de bas khams gsum rnam par rgyal ba ni/ phyag na rdo rje nyid deng?
99a2(rgyud 'grel): rang bzhin gcig pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gdul ba ni/ snang bas snang zhes bstan te me long rkyen gyi gzugs rang la gnyis su snang ba'o/ /de bzhin du sems bskyed pa'i smon lam dang snying rje chen po/ /sems can gzhug pa'i ched
99a3(rgyud 'grel): du ston pa dang/ 'khor ba dang ldan pa dang lam dang dri za'i gzugs dang/ phung po dang skye mched bcu gnyis dang/ khams dang rnam par byang ba'i 'bras bu dang nyon mongs pa dang mang du bstan pa rnams ni/ sems can gzhug pa'i ched yin pas thos

99a6(rgyud 'grel): yin na sangs rgyas ma yin te/ dngos po tha dad du snang zhing shes pa gnyis dang ldan pa'i phyir ro/ /bcom ldan 'das ni log pa'i shes pa dang ste/ sa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' dang khyad par med do/ /de'i phyir de ni sangs rgyas su lta bar
99a7(rgyud 'grel): mi bya'o/ /sprul pa ma yin na snang bar mi rigs so/ /ci'i phyir rgyu mar 'bras bu snang phyir/ ri bong rwa sogs snang bar rig shes bya'o/ /bden de log pa'i shes pa dang ldan na de gnyis 'byung gi /de med pa'i phyir de mi 'byung ngo/ /dngos su sprul yang
99b1(rgyud 'grel): mi lto 'dul ba'i dus la bab pa'i phyir/ de'i rang bzhin der snang pa'o/ /ma sprul yang rang nyid de'i tshe nges 'dul ba la rnam par rgyal bar snang ba'o/ /de nas bka' la bar med pa'i phyir rang gis thos pa dang yang sdud pa pos thos zhes bya'o/ /'dir sems can gdul bya ma
99b2(rgyud 'grel): rtog par ston pa dang sdud pa po tha dad du bya ba med do/ /smon lam dang thugs rje dpag tu med pa'i 'gro don 'byung ba'i phyir thos zhes sbyar ro/ /des na skyon de gnyis mi 'byung ste/ de ni skyon thams cad bral ba'i phyir ro/ /dus kyang de ste de'i tshe de thos gzhan gyi tshe/ gzhan
99b3(rgyud 'grel): thos pa ste bus kyang de'i tshe zhes bstan to/ /'di skad bdag gis thos pa ni e bam mA yA zhes 'byung bas byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis 'byung ba lnga rig dang ye shes lnga dang sgra dang skye mched dang/ khams bco brgyad dang/ g.yo ba dang/ mi g.yo ba dang/ rtsa lnga
99b4(rgyud 'grel): dang dbang dang dga' ba la sogs pa la'ang shes par bya'o/ /da dag bstan pa'i yan lag ni/ phyi nang mthar thug rnam pa gsum ci bzhin min dang ji bzhin sgra/ dgongs pas bshad dang dgongs pa min/ /drang ba'i don dang nges pa'i don/ /phyi ni mi bzad dbyings dang sbyar//
99b5(rgyud 'grel): nang ni rtsa rlung byang chub sems/ rtsa lnga gtum po'i man ngag go /mthar thug mthong lam ye shes te/ /dpe ye shes gnyis med phyag rgya chen po'i lam bcu gnyis ni dngos po bral bden bral ba'i shes ba'o/ /gzhan yang phung po lnga dang/ tshogs drug dang skye mched bcu gnyis dang
99b6(rgyud 'grel): khams dang bag chags khams gsum na bag chags rnams de ni brda min skye bo thal ba'i tshig /dgos pa ma yin zhes su bya/ /shu tra su tra ma nu ha ra dang tan tra yan tra man tra'o/ /byang sems kyi sems can phal pa rnams thugs rje zag bcas thams cad skyob pa'o//
99b7(rgyud 'grel): sngags dang shes pa ma lus yongs su 'dzin rgyud ni 'khor ba rgyud de chos nyid byang chub sems/ /'di yang gnas pa ma lus stong pas 'dzin par byed/ /lung las 'di lta ste/ ji lta ji ltar 'dul 'gyur bas/ sems can ma lus bsad par bya/ /ma byin len
100a1(rgyud 'grel): dang brdzun smra dang/ /de lta de ltar sems can don/ /'dod chags la sogs spang pas spyad/ /sems can kun la phan don du/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa rgyu yi phyir/ /sems can thams cad bsad nas yang/ /de la sdig pa mi gos so//
100a2(rgyud 'grel): sems can kun la phan don du/ sangs rgyas kun la sbyor ba yis/ /gzhan gyi nor rnams phrog na yang/ /de la sdig pa mi gos so/ /'dod chags lta bu bde ba med/ /de ni rgyal ba rnams la phul/ /sems can don du gzhan bud med/ /ston pas
100a3(rgyud 'grel): bsod nams thob? par 'gyur/ /sems can kun la phan don du/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa rgyu yi phyir/ /mi dge bcu sogs spyad pa yang/ /bsod nams rnams mang 'phel zhes gsungs/ /snyoms bar 'jug pa nas bzung ba/ /pha dang ma ni bsad par
100a4(rgyud 'grel): bya/ /rgyal po ngan? pa bkur mi bya/ /bram ze'i grong khyer gzhom par bya/ /des kyang grol bar gsungs pa ste/ /dgongs pa bshad pa zhes ni bya/ /drang pa'i don ni theg pa gsum dang gu ru bstan pa'o/ /yod pas nyan thos rang rgyal rnams ni smo/ /phra rab
100a5(rgyud 'grel): rdzas su 'dod ba nyan thos rnams/ /byang chub sems dpa' de ni byis pa'i rang bzhin no/ /med par zhen cing chags par 'dod pa'i byis pa ste/ /theg pa dman pa log pa'i shes pa ste/ /de mkho je la de'i theg pa bstan/ /ces rgyud las gsungs so//
